3　借着模成，神要得着祂长子同着众子的团体彰显，而完成祂永远的定旨─弗三11。
3.　Through conformation God will obtain the corporate expression of His firstborn Son with His many sons to accomplish His eternal purpose—Eph. 3:11.
二　模成神长子的形像，乃是在生命里得救，脱离己的样式，就是脱离己的彰显和样子─罗五10：
B.　To be conformed to the image of the firstborn Son of God is to be saved in life from self-likeness, that is, from the expression, the appearance, of the self—Rom. 5:10:
1　正如基督是神的具体表现和彰显，己也是撒但的具体表现和彰显─太十六21～24。
1.　As Christ is the embodiment and expression of God, so self is the embodiment and expression of Satan—Matt. 16:21-24.
2　己的彰显就是己的样式；我们都需要在基督的生命里得救，脱离这样的彰显。
2.　The expression of the self is self-likeness; we all need to be saved in the life of Christ from such an expression.
3　当我们得救脱离己的样式，完全模成神的长子基督的形像，我们就在实际上成为神的众子，并且在每一方面具有神众子的样子─来二10。
3.　When we have been saved from our self-likeness and have been fully conformed to the image of Christ as the firstborn Son of God, we will be sons of God in reality, and in every respect we will bear the appearance of God's sons—Heb. 2:10.
三　我们要模成长子的形像，使神得着团体的彰显，就需要蒙拯救脱离乖僻─约壹三2：
C.　In order to be conformed to the image of the firstborn Son for God's corporate expression, we need to be delivered from peculiarity—1 John 3:2:
1　乖僻，我们天然生命最终的彰显，乃是我们弯曲邪僻的特性。
1.　Peculiarity, the final expression of our natural life, is our biased and warped characteristics.
2　我们的乖僻拦阻我们更丰富的经历基督，拦阻我们活基督，并拦阻我们建造为基督的身体─弗三8，四16，腓一20～21上。
2.　Our peculiarity frustrates us from the richer experiences of Christ, from living Christ, and from being built up as the Body of Christ—Eph. 3:8; 4:16; Phil. 1:20-21a.
3　我们里面给基督的据点，已被我们的乖僻狡诈、隐藏的篡夺并据有了；因此，乖僻就是我们里面可怕的敌基督者。
3.　The ground within us for Christ has been subtly and hiddenly usurped and possessed by our peculiarity; thus, peculiarity is a terrible antichrist in our being.
四　我们要模成神长子的形像，就需要凭基督复活的大能模成祂的死─三10：
D.　If we would be conformed to the image of the firstborn Son of God, we need to be con-formed to Christ's death by the power of His resurrection—3:10:
1　基督的死乃是模子，在这模子里我们就被塑造成祂这神长子的形像。
1.　Christ's death is a mold in which we are being shaped into His image as the first-born Son of God.
2　我们若不模成基督的死，我们就不能模成基督的形像。
2.　Unless we are conformed to the death of Christ, we cannot be conformed to the image of Christ.
3　我们历经变化与模成的过程时，我们就是在模成基督的死─林后三18，罗八29，腓三10。
3.　As we are undergoing the process of transformation and conformation, we are being conformed to the death of Christ—2 Cor. 3:18; Rom. 8:29; Phil. 3:10.
五　那灵为我们代求，并且万有为着我们互相效力，使我们完全模成神长子基督的形像─罗八26～29：
E.　The Spirit intercedes for us, and all things are working together for us so that we may be fully conformed to the image of Christ as the firstborn Son—Rom. 8:26-29:
1　基督乃是模型，那灵祷告，使临到我们的每件事都将我们模成这模型，模成神长子的形像。
1.　Christ is the pattern, and the Spirit prays that everything that happens to us will mold us into this pattern, into the image of God's firstborn Son—vv. 26-27.
2　父神是主宰一切的，安排每件事，祂知道什么对我们最有益；父神答应那灵的代求，使万有都互相效力，叫我们得益处，就是模成神长子的形像，作三一神团体的彰显─28～29节。
2.　God the Father is sovereign, arranges everything, and knows what is best for us; He answers the Spirit's intercession by causing all things to work together for good—that we would be conformed to the image of the firstborn Son of God for the corporate expression of the Triune God—vv. 28-29.
六　神已呼召我们，目的是要将我们模成祂儿子的形像，而与神的目的合作的路乃是爱祂─28～29节：
F.　God has called us with the purpose of conforming us to the image of His Son, and the way to cooperate with God in His purpose is to love Him—vv. 28-29:
1　爱神就是与祂合作，与祂合作就是给祂机会在我们里面并在我们身上作出祂的目的─可十二30。
1.　To love God is to cooperate with Him, and to cooperate with Him is to give Him an opportunity to work out His purpose in us and with us—Mark 12:30.
2　我们若爱主，一切就都会为着我们的益处，就是为着我们的模成而效力─罗八29。
2.　If we love the Lord, everything will work together for our profit, that is, for our conformation—Rom. 8:29.
3　万有对我们是益处或是亏损，在于我们对主的爱；秘诀在于爱祂─28节，林前二9。
3.　Whether all things are a profit or loss to us depends on our love for the Lord; the secret is to love Him—v. 28; 1 Cor. 2:9.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
第十二篇　借着那爱我们的，在苦楚、患难、苦难、困苦、以及一切境遇中得胜有余
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
读经：罗八18，31～39，五5，17，21
壹　“在这一切的事上，我们已经得胜有余了”─罗八37：
一　“这一切的事”指苦楚、患难和困苦─18，31节。
二　“得胜有余，”意思是得胜中的得胜，是最高度的得胜─37节：
1　神给的得胜只有一种，就是得胜有余的得胜。
2　凡是仅仅的得胜，凡是刚刚的得胜，都不是主赐给的得胜。
3　主给的得胜，总是“超越的得胜”（罗马八章三十七节里“得胜有余”的原文意。）─引用经文
三　我们不是自己得胜，乃是在基督的得胜里，得胜有余─林前十五57：
1　基督借着祂的复活，胜过了神的仇敌撒但、世界、罪和死─来二14，徒二24，启一17～18。
2　基督的复活乃是祂的得胜，祂的得胜要为我们这些有分于祂复活的人，在复活中完成终极完成的得胜─林前十五54，腓三10。
3　基督的得胜必须成为我们的经历─林前十五57：
a　基督的得胜不该只是一件完成的事实给我们接受，也必须借着复活的基督这赐生命的灵，与我们的灵联结成为一灵，而成为我们日常的经历─45节下，六17。
b　不管是患难，是困苦，是逼迫，我们不只该在其中得胜，还能在其中得胜有余；这是神为我们所定规的经历─罗八35～37。
四　我们在生命中作王，就能在一切境遇中得胜─五17，21，八31～39，参林前十五54～57。
1　在生命中作王就是像君王一样掌权─启二十4，6，二二5：
a　作王就是征服、制伏并管治撒但、世界、肉体、我们自己、和我们环境上的一切遭遇─约壹五4。
b　我们基督徒的生命不仅该是胜利、得胜的生命；也该是君尊、作王的生命─五17，21。
2　在生命中作王乃是在生命和性情上成为神，但无分于祂的神格─约一12～13：
a　在宇宙中，惟有神作王，也只有祂是君王；但我们是这位君王的儿女，也能在祂的生命中作王─罗五17。
b　神作王，我们也作王；我们既如同神一样作王，就借着在生命中作王而在生命和性情上成为神，只是无分于祂的神格─八16，西三4，彼后一4。
c　当我们在生命中作王，我们就在环境的艰难和苦难上得胜有余；这是因着有神帮助我们─罗八31，34。
五　在一切的境遇中，我们必须在与基督的得胜里，超越一切：
1　我们能超越，因为我们在基督的复活和升天里与祂联合，并与祂一同坐在诸天界里；这才是超越一切─弗二5～6。
2　我们远超过一切执政的、掌权的、有能的、主治的、以及一切受称之名，不但是今世的，连来世的也都在内─一20～23节。
3　今天我们能在基督的得胜里，与祂一同过超越一切的生活─二5～6。
贰　“借着那爱我们的”，我们已经得胜有余了─罗八37：
一　因着神对我们不变的爱，和基督已为我们成就一切的事实，患难或逼迫都不能压制或击败我们；反而借着那爱我们的，我们胜过且征服这一切而有余─37节。
二　罗马八章里基督的爱是为着受苦的人─18节：
1　无论我们的问题是什么，答覆总是基督的爱─37节。
2　是基督的爱叫我们能胜过一切的患难和困苦。
三　我们不是被击败，乃是借着那爱我们的，已经得胜有余了─37节：
1　我们被治死，人看我们如将宰的羊─36节。
2　然而借着那爱我们的，在这一切的事上，我们已经得胜有余了。
3　爱我们的主，在这一切的事上，已经得胜有余了；这该是所有基督徒所共有的经历─37节，约壹五4。
4　借着那爱我们的，我们不仅得胜，也能成为得胜者，胜过一切消极的事物，甚至死亡─徒二24，启一17下～18。
四　惟有一种爱是真实的，这爱乃是三一神分赐的结果─罗八35，39，十五30：
1　因为那灵有爱的属性，我们越在祂的分赐之下，就越有真实的爱─约壹四8，16。
2　事实上，那灵越分赐到我们里面，我们就越在被神圣的爱所构成的意义上成为爱─罗十五30，弗四15～16。
3　这样我们就会有作那灵彰显的爱，也会用这爱回应别人─加五22。
五　神的爱浇灌在我们心里，乃是神素质的事─罗五5：
1　因为神的爱已经浇灌在我们心里，每个信徒的心都是爱的心。
2　我们在神的爱里经历并享受神是父，乃是经历并享受那是神素质之性质的爱，分赐到我们心里。
六　在以弗所三章十九节保罗说到基督那超越知识的爱：─引用经文
1　基督的爱是超越知识的爱；然而我们能借着经历认识这爱。
2　基督是不可度量的，祂的爱也是不可度量的─18～19节：
a　我们若以目前所经历基督那不可度量的爱，与将来所要经历的相比，就如一滴水与大海相比一样。
b　基督的宇宙量度和祂不可度量的爱，犹如广大无垠的大海，让我们来经历─18～19节。
七　以弗所四章十五至十六节所题到的爱─神内在的本质─乃是在基督里面神的爱，成了在我们里面基督的爱，这爱不仅使我们能爱，也使我们借着是爱之三一神─神的爱、基督的爱和那灵的爱─的分赐而成为爱─罗八39，35，十五30。
八　神在基督里永远的爱，是在我们以上展开的旌旗，陈列、展示我们蒙神所爱的人始终是得胜有余的─八37。
九　“你将要受的苦你不用怕”（启二10上），因为借着那爱我们的─我们所爱的主耶稣基督，“万主之主，万王之王，”（十七14，）在这一切的事上，我们会得胜有余。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
CHAPTERS FIVE THROUGH EIGHT OF ROMANS— THE KERNEL OF THE BIBLE
Message Twelve
More Than Conquering in Sufferings, Tribulations, Afflictions, Anguish, and All Circumstances through the One Who Loves Us
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
Scripture Reading: Rom. 8:18, 31-39; 5:5, 17, 21
I.　"In all these things we more than conquer"—Rom. 8:37:
A.　These things refers to sufferings, tribulation, and anguish—vv. 18, 31.
B.　More than conquer means a victory among victories, the highest form of victory—v. 37:
1.　God gives only one kind of victory—the victory that more than conquers.
2.　Any victory that barely makes it is not a victory from the Lord.
3.　The Lord's victory is always one that "super overcomes" (the meaning of the Greek word rendered "more than conquer" in Romans 8:37).
C.　We do not overcome in ourselves; we more than conquer in Christ's victory—1 Cor. 15:57:
1.　Through His resurrection Christ was victorious over Satan, God's enemy, over the world, over sin, and over death—Heb. 2:14; Acts 2:24; Rev. 1:17-18.
2.　Christ's resurrection was His victory, which will accomplish the ultimate and complete victory in resurrection for us who participate in His resurrection—1 Cor. 15:54; Phil. 3:10.
3.　We need Christ's victory to become our experience—1 Cor. 15:57:
a.　The victory of the Lord Jesus should not only be an accomplished fact for us; it should also become our daily experience through the union with the resurrected Christ as the life-giving Spirit with our spirit—v. 45b; 6:17.
b.　Whether we encounter tribulation, anguish, or persecution, we should not only conquer in it but more than conquer in it; this is the experience that God has ordained for us—Rom 8:35-37.
D.　When we reign in life, we can overcome in all circumstances—5:17, 21; 8:31-39; cf. 1 Cor. 15:54-57:
1.　To reign in life is to rule as kings—Rev. 20:4, 6; 22:5:
a.　To reign is to conquer, subdue, and rule over Satan, the world, the flesh, ourselves, and all our environmental circumstances—1 John 5:4.
b.　Our Christian life should not only be a victorious and overcoming life; it should also be a kingly and reigning life—5:17, 21.
2.　To reign in life is to be God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead—John 1:12-13:
a.　In the universe only God reigns and only He is the King, but we as the children of this King can also reign in His life—Rom. 5:17.
b.　Since we reign as God does, by reigning in life we become God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead—8:16; Col. 3:4; 2 Pet. 1:4.
c.　When we reign in life, we more than conquer the environmental hardships and sufferings by having God, who is for us—Rom. 8:31, 34.
E.　We need to be all-transcending in our overcoming with Christ in all circumstances:
1.　We can be transcendent because we are joined with Christ in His resurrection and ascension and are seated with Him in the heavenlies; this is to be transcendent over all things— Eph. 2:5-6.
2.　We are far above all rule and authority and power and lordship and every name that is named not only in this age but also in that which is to come—1:21-23.
3.　Today we can live an all-transcending life with Christ in His victory—2:5-6.
II.　We more than conquer "through Him who loved us"—Rom. 8:37:
A.　Because of God's unchanging love for us and the fact that Christ has accomplished everything on our behalf, neither tribulation nor persecution can suppress or defeat us; rather, in all these things we more than overcome and conquer through Him who loved us—v. 37.
B.　The love of Christ in Romans 8 is for those who are suffering—v. 18:
1.　Whatever problem we may have, the answer is always the love of Christ—v. 37.
2.　It is the love of Christ that enables us to overcome all tribulation and anguish.
C.　Instead of being defeated, we more than conquer through the One who loves us—v. 37:
1.　We are being put to death and are accounted as sheep for slaughter—v. 36.
2.　Nevertheless, in all these things we more than conquer through Him who loved us.
3.　Our Lord who loves us has more than conquered all these things; this should be the common experience of all Christians—v. 37; 1 John 5:4.
4.　Through our loving One we not only conquer—we can be conquerors, conquering all negative things, even death—Acts 2:24; Rev. 1:17b-18.
D.　Only one kind of love is genuine, and that is the love that is the issue of the dispensing of the Triune God—Rom. 8:35, 39; 15:30:
1.　Because the Spirit has the attribute of love, the more we are under His dispensing, the more genuine love we have—1 John 4:8, 16.
2.　Actually, the more the Spirit is dispensed into us, the more we become love in the sense of being constituted with the divine love—Rom. 15:30; Eph. 4:15-16.
3.　Then we will have the love that is the expression of the Spirit, and we will respond to others with love—Gal. 5:22.
E.　The pouring out of the love of God into our hearts is a matter of the essence of God—Rom. 5:5:
1.　Because the love of God has been poured out into our hearts, the heart of every believer is a heart of love.
2.　In our experience and enjoyment of God as the Father in His love, we experience and enjoy the dispensing of love as the nature of God's essence into our hearts.
F.　In Ephesians 3:19 Paul speaks of the knowledge-surpassing love of Christ:
1.　The love of Christ surpasses knowledge, yet we can know it by experiencing it.
2.　Just as Christ is immeasurable, so His love is immeasurable—vv. 18-19:
a.　If we compare what we have so far experienced of the immeasurable love of Christ to all that there is to experience, it is like comparing a raindrop to the ocean.
b.　Christ in His universal dimensions and in His immeasurable love is like a vast, limitless ocean for us to experience—vv. 18-19.
G.　The love mentioned in Ephesians 4:15-16—the inner substance of God—is the love of God in Christ that becomes the love of Christ in us, not only enabling us to love but also causing us to become love through the dispensing of the Triune God of love—the love of God, the love of Christ, and the love of the Spirit—Rom. 8:39, 35; 15:30.
H.　God's everlasting love in Christ is a banner spreading over us, displaying and exhibiting that we who are loved by God are more than conquerors—8:37.
I.　"Do not fear the things that you are about to suffer" (Rev. 2:10a), for in all these things we will more than conquer through the One who loves us—our beloved Lord Jesus Christ, "Lord of lords and King of kings" (17:14).

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第十二篇　借着那爱我们的，在苦楚、患难、苦难、困苦、以及一切境遇中得胜有余
More Than Conquering in Sufferings, Tribulations, Afflictions, Anguish, and All Circumstances through the One Who Loves Us
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
读经：罗八18，31～39，五5，17，21
壹　“在这一切的事上，我们已经得胜有余了”─罗八37：
I.　"In all these things we more than conquer"—Rom. 8:37:
一　“这一切的事”指苦楚、患难和困苦─18，31节。
A.　These things refers to sufferings, tribulation, and anguish—vv. 18, 31.
二　“得胜有余，”意思是得胜中的得胜，是最高度的得胜─37节：
B.　More than conquer means a victory among victories, the highest form of victory—v. 37:
1　神给的得胜只有一种，就是得胜有余的得胜。
1.　God gives only one kind of victory—the victory that more than conquers.
2　凡是仅仅的得胜，凡是刚刚的得胜，都不是主赐给的得胜。
2.　Any victory that barely makes it is not a victory from the Lord.
3　主给的得胜，总是“超越的得胜”（罗马八章三十七节里“得胜有余”的原文意。）─引用经文
3.　The Lord's victory is always one that "super overcomes" (the meaning of the Greek word rendered "more than conquer" in Romans 8:37).
三　我们不是自己得胜，乃是在基督的得胜里，得胜有余─林前十五57：
C.　We do not overcome in ourselves; we more than conquer in Christ's victory—1 Cor. 15:57:
1　基督借着祂的复活，胜过了神的仇敌撒但、世界、罪和死─来二14，徒二24，启一17～18。
1.　Through His resurrection Christ was victorious over Satan, God's enemy, over the world, over sin, and over death—Heb. 2:14; Acts 2:24; Rev. 1:17-18.
2　基督的复活乃是祂的得胜，祂的得胜要为我们这些有分于祂复活的人，在复活中完成终极完成的得胜─林前十五54，腓三10。
2.　Christ's resurrection was His victory, which will accomplish the ultimate and complete victory in resurrection for us who participate in His resurrection—1 Cor. 15:54; Phil. 3:10.
3　基督的得胜必须成为我们的经历─林前十五57：
3.　We need Christ's victory to become our experience—1 Cor. 15:57:
a　基督的得胜不该只是一件完成的事实给我们接受，也必须借着复活的基督这赐生命的灵，与我们的灵联结成为一灵，而成为我们日常的经历─45节下，六17。
a.　The victory of the Lord Jesus should not only be an accomplished fact for us; it should also become our daily experience through the union with the resurrected Christ as the life-giving Spirit with our spirit—v. 45b; 6:17.
b　不管是患难，是困苦，是逼迫，我们不只该在其中得胜，还能在其中得胜有余；这是神为我们所定规的经历─罗八35～37。
b.　Whether we encounter tribulation, anguish, or persecution, we should not only conquer in it but more than conquer in it; this is the experience that God has ordained for us—Rom 8:35-37.
四　我们在生命中作王，就能在一切境遇中得胜─五17，21，八31～39，参林前十五54～57。
D.　When we reign in life, we can overcome in all circumstances—5:17, 21; 8:31-39; cf. 1 Cor. 15:54-57:
1　在生命中作王就是像君王一样掌权─启二十4，6，二二5：
1.　To reign in life is to rule as kings—Rev. 20:4, 6; 22:5:
a　作王就是征服、制伏并管治撒但、世界、肉体、我们自己、和我们环境上的一切遭遇─约壹五4。
a.　To reign is to conquer, subdue, and rule over Satan, the world, the flesh, ourselves, and all our environmental circumstances—1 John 5:4.
b　我们基督徒的生命不仅该是胜利、得胜的生命；也该是君尊、作王的生命─五17，21。
b.　Our Christian life should not only be a victorious and overcoming life; it should also be a kingly and reigning life—5:17, 21.
2　在生命中作王乃是在生命和性情上成为神，但无分于祂的神格─约一12～13：
2.　To reign in life is to be God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead—John 1:12-13:
a　在宇宙中，惟有神作王，也只有祂是君王；但我们是这位君王的儿女，也能在祂的生命中作王─罗五17。
a.　In the universe only God reigns and only He is the King, but we as the children of this King can also reign in His life—Rom. 5:17.
b　神作王，我们也作王；我们既如同神一样作王，就借着在生命中作王而在生命和性情上成为神，只是无分于祂的神格─八16，西三4，彼后一4。
b.　Since we reign as God does, by reigning in life we become God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead—8:16; Col. 3:4; 2 Pet. 1:4.
c　当我们在生命中作王，我们就在环境的艰难和苦难上得胜有余；这是因着有神帮助我们─罗八31，34。
c.　When we reign in life, we more than conquer the environmental hardships and sufferings by having God, who is for us—Rom. 8:31, 34.
五　在一切的境遇中，我们必须在与基督的得胜里，超越一切：
E.　We need to be all-transcending in our overcoming with Christ in all circumstances:
1　我们能超越，因为我们在基督的复活和升天里与祂联合，并与祂一同坐在诸天界里；这才是超越一切─弗二5～6。
1.　We can be transcendent because we are joined with Christ in His resurrection and ascension and are seated with Him in the heavenlies; this is to be transcendent over all things— Eph. 2:5-6.
2　我们远超过一切执政的、掌权的、有能的、主治的、以及一切受称之名，不但是今世的，连来世的也都在内─一20～23节。
2.　We are far above all rule and authority and power and lordship and every name that is named not only in this age but also in that which is to come—1:21-23.
3　今天我们能在基督的得胜里，与祂一同过超越一切的生活─二5～6。
3.　Today we can live an all-transcending life with Christ in His victory—2:5-6.
贰　“借着那爱我们的”，我们已经得胜有余了─罗八37：
II.　We more than conquer "through Him who loved us"—Rom. 8:37:
一　因着神对我们不变的爱，和基督已为我们成就一切的事实，患难或逼迫都不能压制或击败我们；反而借着那爱我们的，我们胜过且征服这一切而有余─37节。
A.　Because of God's unchanging love for us and the fact that Christ has accomplished everything on our behalf, neither tribulation nor persecution can suppress or defeat us; rather, in all these things we more than overcome and conquer through Him who loved us—v. 37.
二　罗马八章里基督的爱是为着受苦的人─18节：
B.　The love of Christ in Romans 8 is for those who are suffering—v. 18:
1　无论我们的问题是什么，答覆总是基督的爱─37节。
1.　Whatever problem we may have, the answer is always the love of Christ—v. 37.
2　是基督的爱叫我们能胜过一切的患难和困苦。
2.　It is the love of Christ that enables us to overcome all tribulation and anguish.
三　我们不是被击败，乃是借着那爱我们的，已经得胜有余了─37节：
C.　Instead of being defeated, we more than conquer through the One who loves us—v. 37:
1　我们被治死，人看我们如将宰的羊─36节。
1.　We are being put to death and are accounted as sheep for slaughter—v. 36.
2　然而借着那爱我们的，在这一切的事上，我们已经得胜有余了。
2.　Nevertheless, in all these things we more than conquer through Him who loved us.
3　爱我们的主，在这一切的事上，已经得胜有余了；这该是所有基督徒所共有的经历─37节，约壹五4。
3.　Our Lord who loves us has more than conquered all these things; this should be the common experience of all Christians—v. 37; 1 John 5:4.
4　借着那爱我们的，我们不仅得胜，也能成为得胜者，胜过一切消极的事物，甚至死亡─徒二24，启一17下～18。
4.　Through our loving One we not only conquer—we can be conquerors, conquering all negative things, even death—Acts 2:24; Rev. 1:17b-18.
四　惟有一种爱是真实的，这爱乃是三一神分赐的结果─罗八35，39，十五30：
D.　Only one kind of love is genuine, and that is the love that is the issue of the dispensing of the Triune God—Rom. 8:35, 39; 15:30:
1　因为那灵有爱的属性，我们越在祂的分赐之下，就越有真实的爱─约壹四8，16。
1.　Because the Spirit has the attribute of love, the more we are under His dispensing, the more genuine love we have—1 John 4:8, 16.
2　事实上，那灵越分赐到我们里面，我们就越在被神圣的爱所构成的意义上成为爱─罗十五30，弗四15～16。
2.　Actually, the more the Spirit is dispensed into us, the more we become love in the sense of being constituted with the divine love—Rom. 15:30; Eph. 4:15-16.
3　这样我们就会有作那灵彰显的爱，也会用这爱回应别人─加五22。
3.　Then we will have the love that is the expression of the Spirit, and we will respond to others with love—Gal. 5:22.
五　神的爱浇灌在我们心里，乃是神素质的事─罗五5：
E.　The pouring out of the love of God into our hearts is a matter of the essence of God—Rom. 5:5:
1　因为神的爱已经浇灌在我们心里，每个信徒的心都是爱的心。
1.　Because the love of God has been poured out into our hearts, the heart of every believer is a heart of love.
2　我们在神的爱里经历并享受神是父，乃是经历并享受那是神素质之性质的爱，分赐到我们心里。
2.　In our experience and enjoyment of God as the Father in His love, we experience and enjoy the dispensing of love as the nature of God's essence into our hearts.
六　在以弗所三章十九节保罗说到基督那超越知识的爱：─引用经文
F.　In Ephesians 3:19 Paul speaks of the knowledge-surpassing love of Christ:
1　基督的爱是超越知识的爱；然而我们能借着经历认识这爱。
1.　The love of Christ surpasses knowledge, yet we can know it by experiencing it.
2　基督是不可度量的，祂的爱也是不可度量的─18～19节：
2.　Just as Christ is immeasurable, so His love is immeasurable—vv. 18-19:
a　我们若以目前所经历基督那不可度量的爱，与将来所要经历的相比，就如一滴水与大海相比一样。
a.　If we compare what we have so far experienced of the immeasurable love of Christ to all that there is to experience, it is like comparing a raindrop to the ocean.
b　基督的宇宙量度和祂不可度量的爱，犹如广大无垠的大海，让我们来经历─18～19节。
b.　Christ in His universal dimensions and in His immeasurable love is like a vast, limitless ocean for us to experience—vv. 18-19.
七　以弗所四章十五至十六节所题到的爱─神内在的本质─乃是在基督里面神的爱，成了在我们里面基督的爱，这爱不仅使我们能爱，也使我们借着是爱之三一神─神的爱、基督的爱和那灵的爱─的分赐而成为爱─罗八39，35，十五30。
G.　The love mentioned in Ephesians 4:15-16—the inner substance of God—is the love of God in Christ that becomes the love of Christ in us, not only enabling us to love but also causing us to become love through the dispensing of the Triune God of love—the love of God, the love of Christ, and the love of the Spirit—Rom. 8:39, 35; 15:30.
八　神在基督里永远的爱，是在我们以上展开的旌旗，陈列、展示我们蒙神所爱的人始终是得胜有余的─八37。
H.　God's everlasting love in Christ is a banner spreading over us, displaying and exhibiting that we who are loved by God are more than conquerors—8:37.
九　“你将要受的苦你不用怕”（启二10上），因为借着那爱我们的─我们所爱的主耶稣基督，“万主之主，万王之王，”（十七14，）在这一切的事上，我们会得胜有余。
I.　"Do not fear the things that you are about to suffer" (Rev. 2:10a), for in all these things we will more than conquer through the One who loves us—our beloved Lord Jesus Christ, "Lord of lords and King of kings" (17:14).

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
第十三篇　学习享受基督作生命之灵的律的秘诀，以活在新约禧年的实际里
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
读经：利二五8～17，赛六一1～3，路四16～22，罗八2，16
壹　利未记二十五章八至十七节里的禧年，作为预言记载在以赛亚六十一章一至三节，实际的应验在路加四章十六至二十二节：─引用经文
一　禧年有两项主要的福分，就是各人归回失去的产业，以及从奴役得着释放─利二五8～17：
1　每一个卖了他所分得美地一分产业的，在禧年要归回自己的产业，而无须付赎价（10，13，28）；并且凡卖了自己作奴仆的，要重得自由，归回本家（39～41）。─引用经文
2　归回自己的产业以及得自由归回本家，表征在新约的禧年里，信徒已经归回神，就是他们所失去神圣的产业，并且从一切捆绑得释放，回到召会，就是他们神圣的家─弗一13～14，约八32，36，参诗六八5～6。
二　在旧约的预表里，禧年持续一年之久，其应验却是指整个新约时代，恩典时代，这是神悦纳归回的罪囚的时候（赛四九8，路十五17～24，林后六2），也是那些在罪的捆绑下受压制的人享受神救恩之释放的时候（罗七14～八2）。─引用经文
贰　新约时代就是狂喜时代，基督徒乃是狂喜的人；若是我们从来没有在神面前狂喜过，就表明我们对神的享受不够─林后六2，五13～15，徒十一5，二二17，诗四三4上，五一12，彼前一8，赛十二3～6：
一　“禧年”的意思就是无忧无虑、无牵无挂、无缺无乏、无病无灾，什么难处都没有，什么都是好处；因此，一切应心，万事如意，逍遥自在，狂喜欢腾─腓四6～7，11～13，诗一〇三1～5。
二　我们必须接受主耶稣在我们里面作真正的禧年；我们得着了祂，就有神作我们的产业，并且能蒙拯救脱离罪和撒但的辖制，而有真正的自由与安息─徒二六18，弗一13～14，西一12，太十一28，约八32，36。
三　我们接受基督作我们的救主和生命时，祂就作为生命之灵的律进到我们里面作我们的禧年，但我们若没有让基督活在我们里面，也不凭基督活着，我们就还没有实际的活在禧年里─利二五11～12，罗八2：
1　我们的心若放在主以外任何的人事物上，乃是拜偶像，结局都是苦恼─约壹五21，参结十四3，5，六9。
2　我们若让基督活在我们里面，并凭祂活着，一切就都应心如意；否则一切就都是难处，凡事都没有禧年。
四　只有当这位包罗万有的基督给我们得着了，给我们享受了，我们才可能一切应心，万事如意；不是外面的人事物，乃是里面的基督，能叫我们安稳无忧的面对各样的环境─腓三8～9，四5～8，11～13：
1　亚当没有接受生命树，就失去他享受神的分；世上一切不信的人都失去神作他们的产业和享受，并且将自己的肢体卖给罪，成为罪的奴仆─弗二12，罗七14，六19。
2　人生不过是劳苦愁烦，转眼成空；人生的实况乃是虚空的虚空，空中之空─都是捕风─诗九十10，七三14，16～17，25，传一2～11，14。
五　信徒享受基督作恩典的禧年，要带进千年国里对禧年完满的享受，以及在新天新地新耶路撒冷里最完满的享受─腓三14，启二二1～2上。
六　利未记二十五章十节的“禧年”这辞，意思是“呼喊的时候”，或“吹公羊角的时候”；我们传福音就是吹公羊角，向世人宣扬：“看哪，现在正是最可蒙悦纳的时候；看哪，现在正是拯救的日子”─林后六2，赛六一1～3：
1　神造人时，定意要将自己在基督里给人，作人的产业，人的基业（创二9，十三12～15，诗十六5，九十1）；然而，人堕落了，在堕落中人失去神作为产业（创三24，四16，弗二12），将自己卖给罪、撒但和世界，受其奴役（约八34，罗七14下，加四8，多三3，约壹五19下）。─引用经文
2　堕落的人没有真实的住处；他们都是漂泊、流浪、无家可归的，因为神是人真正的居所─诗九十1，创二八17～19，约十五4，太十一28。
3　神新约的救恩乃是将堕落的人带回归神，作他神圣的产业（加三14，弗一14，西一12，路十五12～24），释放人脱离罪、撒但和世界的奴役（约八32，罗六6，14，八2，来二14～15，约十二31），并将人恢复到他神圣的家庭，就是神的家里（加六10，弗二19），使他享受神恩典里的交通（林后十三14）。─引用经文
叁　我们惟有享受基督作生命之灵的律，才能得着释放，才有真自由，使我们活在新约禧年的实际里（罗八2，路四16～22）；惟有享受祂的人能不犯罪，而有真自由，过一个自由、释放、脱离辖制的生活─约八36：
一　如果我们享受主不够，就在许多事上还会受捆绑；立志没有用，我们一定要不断的来到主这里，吃祂并享受祂─林前一9，启二7，赛五五1～2。
二　在我们的生活和事奉上，我们必须是走享受基督作生命树的路的人（约六57，63，林后三3～6，约壹五16上）；创世记里的生命树，是我们灵里生命之灵的律，善恶树是我们肉体里罪与死的律（二9，罗八2，6）。─引用经文
三　惟有借着将心思置于灵，享受基督作生命之灵的律的人才不实行罪，才有真自由；我们借着操练灵接触那在我们灵里的主作为生命之灵的律时，就享受基督作禧年无数丰富的方面─约八11～12，24，28，31～36，罗八2，6，16，腓一19。
四　基督在我们里面作禧年，释放我们脱离贫穷、被掳、瞎眼和受压制─传一2，14，三11，腓三8，彼后二22，路十二21，启三17。
五　保罗是“打开”生命之灵的律“开关”的人；他打开这开关乃是借着在他的灵里，出于他对主起初的爱事奉神─罗一9，五5，八35～39，启二4～5：
1　用起初的爱爱主，就是在一切事物上让祂居首位，尊重祂是我们生活中的一切─西一18下，10，林前二9～10。
2　在我们身上，神进来了，神再出去，那就是我们对祂的事奉；我们乃是在众召会中与基督同工，在那里将我们起初的爱给祂─歌七12，林后六1上，腓三3，可十二30。
六　神的救恩使我们有真自由；我们的产业是神，我们的自由来自我们对神的享受：
1　人若不享受神，是不会有真自由的；自由就是释放，就是脱开一切捆绑、一切重担、一切压制、和一切辖制─约八32，36，加五1，林后三17：
a　人若没有神，那么他在神以外所尝试享受的一切都是狗食、废物、粪土─腓三7～9，参彼后二22。
b　撒但称为别西布尔（Beelzebul），意“粪堆之王”；这名源自“别西卜”（Be?elzebub），意“苍蝇之王”；撒但专门带着罪人像苍蝇一样吃粪─太十25，十二24，27，王下一2。
2　我们人生里的每一件事，都可能是我们的辖制；在每一件事之下我们都可能作奴隶；首先撒但把我们俘掳了，然后他就来住在我们里面，作我们犯罪的主动者、主使者；结果他就成了我们非法的主人，我们就作了他的俘虏，使我们好事不作，专作犯罪的事─约八34，罗七14，约壹五19。
七　我们已经被基督征服，成了祂的俘虏，我们在我们的职事里为着基督的行动，乃是庆祝基督的得胜，使祂得着凯旋的荣耀（林后二12～14）；基督拯救我们脱离撒但的掳掠（诗六八18，弗四8）；现今我们既属于祂，惟有祂是我们的夫子与主人（太二三8，出二一6），我们乃是“真自由了”（约八36，参林后十3～5）。─引用经文
肆　禧年的生活乃是享受基督作生命之灵的律的生活，就是享受神作我们的基业和真自由的生活：
一　得释放脱离人生的三种劳苦─作好人的劳苦、挂虑的劳苦、和受苦的劳苦─惟一的路，是以基督作我们的享受、满足和安息─罗七24～八2，腓四5～7，林后十二9。
二　基督徒的生活应该是满了享受主的生活，满了喜乐和赞美的生活；当我们完满享受主时，祂就成了我们的禧年；得胜生活的腔调乃是一直喜乐并感谢赞美神的腔调─帖前五16～18，诗五十14，23，一〇六12。
三　禧年的生活，就是我们在任何情况中都取用神自己，取用基督自己的生活；然后祂就在我们里面作主因、作中心，带领我们克服人生一切的困扰─约六16～21，西一17下，18下。
四　保罗学得活在禧年里的秘诀，就是在各种的环境里赢得基督（腓三8～9）；因着一切都在祂的主宰之下，所以我们应该祷告说，“主阿，求你充满我，得着我，占有我；不管外面情况如何，我就是要享受你”─四5～7，11～13。
五　我们都该有一个心─爱神、寻求神、活神、并被神构成，使我们成为祂的彰显；我们也该有一条路─三一神自己作为内里生命之灵的律连同其神圣的性能─耶三二39。
伍　在罗马八章里经历并享受生命之灵的律作禧年的实际，乃是十二至十六章所展示之基督身体─得成全之神人的团体生活─的实际；这实际终极完成于新耶路撒冷：
一　神完成祂的经纶，是借着将祂自己分赐到我们里面作生命之灵的律─八2，6，10～11，启二二1～2上。
二　生命之灵的律将我们构成基督身体具有各种功用的肢体─西二19，弗四11，16，罗十二4～8。
三　借着我们里面生命之灵的律自发自动的功用，我们就能认识神、得着神、因而把神活出来，使我们被神构成，得以成为祂的扩增和扩大，作祂的丰满，使祂得着彰显─弗一22～23，三19～21。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
CHAPTERS FIVE THROUGH EIGHT OF ROMANS— THE KERNEL OF THE BIBLE
Message Thirteen
Learning the Secret of Enjoying Christ as the Law of the Spirit of Life to Live in the Reality of the New Testament Jubilee
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
Scripture Reading: Lev. 25:8-17; Isa. 61:1-3; Luke 4:16-22; Rom. 8:2, 16
I.　The year of jubilee in Leviticus 25:8-17 is recorded as a prophecy in Isaiah 61:1-3 and fulfilled in reality in Luke 4:16-22:
A.　In the year of jubilee there were two main blessings: the returning of every man to his lost possession and the liberation from slavery—Lev. 25:8-17:
1.　In the year of jubilee everyone who had sold his possession, his allotted portion of the good land, was returned to it without paying anything to redeem it (vv. 10, 13, 28), and everyone who had sold himself into slavery regained his freedom and returned to his family (vv. 39-41).
2.　Returning to one's possession and being freed and returning to one's family signify that in the New Testament jubilee the believers have returned to God as their lost divine possession, have been released from all bondage, and have returned to the church as their divine family—Eph. 1:13-14; John 8:32, 36; cf. Psa. 68:5-6.
B.　In the Old Testament type the jubilee lasted for one year, but in the fulfillment it refers to the entire New Testament age, the age of grace, as the time when God accepts the returned captives of sin (Isa. 49:8; Luke 15:17-24; 2 Cor. 6:2) and when those oppressed under the bondage of sin enjoy the release of God's salvation (Rom. 7:14—8:2).
II.　The New Testament age is an age of ecstasy, and a Christian is a person in ecstasy; if we have never been in ecstasy before God, this shows that we do not have a sufficient enjoyment of God—2 Cor. 6:2; 5:13-15; Acts 11:5; 22:17; Psa. 43:4a; 51:12; 1 Pet. 1:8; Isa. 12:3-6:
A.　Jubilee means having no worry or anxiety, no concern or care, no lack or shortage, no sickness or calamity, and no problems whatsoever but, rather, having all benefits; hence, all things are pleas-ant and satisfying to our heart, and we are free from anxiety, at ease, excited, and exultant— Phil. 4:6-7, 11-13; Psa. 103:1-5.
B.　We must receive the Lord Jesus as the real jubilee in us; if we have Him, we have God as our possession and can be delivered from the bondage of sin and Satan to have real freedom and rest—Acts 26:18; Eph. 1:13-14; Col. 1:12; Matt. 11:28; John 8:32, 36.
C.　When we receive Christ as our Savior and life, He comes into us as the law of the Spirit of life to be our jubilee, but unless we allow Him to live in us and unless we live by Him, we are not practically living in the jubilee—Lev. 25:11-12; Rom. 8:2:
1.　If our heart is set on any person, thing, or matter other than the Lord, this is idolatry, and the end is wretchedness—1 John 5:21; cf. Ezek. 14:3, 5; 6:9.
2.　If we allow Christ to live in us and we live by Him, everything is to our satisfaction; otherwise, everything is a problem, and nothing is a jubilee.
D.　Everything can be satisfying to us only after we have gained the all-inclusive Christ as our enjoyment; it is not outward persons, matters, or things but Christ within us who enables us to be calm and free of worries as we face all kinds of situations—Phil. 3:8-9; 4:5-8, 11-13:
1.　Adam lost his portion of the enjoyment of God when he did not take the tree of life; all the unbelieving people of the world have lost God as their possession and enjoyment and have sold their members to sin in order to become slaves of sin—Eph. 2:12; Rom. 7:14; 6:19.
2.　Human life is nothing but labor and sorrow and will soon be gone; the true condition of human life is vanity of vanities, emptiness of emptinesses—a chasing after wind—Psa. 90:10; 73:14, 16-17, 25; Eccl. 1:2-11, 14.
E.　The believers' enjoyment of Christ as the jubilee of grace will issue in the full enjoyment of the jubilee in the millennium and in the fullest enjoyment in the New Jerusalem in the new heaven and new earth—Phil. 3:14; Rev. 22:1-2a.
F.　The word jubilee in Leviticus 25:10 means "a time of shouting," or "a time of the trumpeting of the ram's horn"; our preaching of the gospel is our blowing of the trumpet to proclaim to the world, "Behold, now is the well-acceptable time; behold, now is the day of salvation"—2 Cor. 6:2; Isa. 61:1-3:
1.　When God created man, He intended to give Himself in Christ to man as man's possession, man's inheritance (Gen. 2:9; 13:12-15; Psa. 16:5; 90:1); however, man became fallen, and in the fall man lost God as his possession (Gen. 3:24; 4:16; Eph. 2:12) and sold himself into slavery under sin, Satan, and the world (John 8:34; Rom. 7:14b; Gal. 4:8; Titus 3:3; 1 John 5:19b).
2.　Fallen people have no real dwelling place; they are drifting about and wandering without a home, because God is man's real dwelling place—Psa. 90:1; Gen. 28:17-19; John 15:4; Matt. 11:28.
3.　God's New Testament salvation brings fallen man back to God as his divine possession (Gal. 3:14; Eph. 1:14; Col. 1:12; Luke 15:12-24), releases man from slavery under sin, Satan, and the world (John 8:32; Rom. 6:6, 14; 8:2; Heb. 2:14-15; John 12:31), and restores man to his divine family, the household of God (Gal. 6:10; Eph. 2:19), that he may enjoy fellowship in God's grace (2 Cor. 13:14).
III.　We can be released and have real freedom only by enjoying Christ as the law of the Spirit of life so that we may live in the reality of the New Testament jubilee (Rom. 8:2; Luke 4:16-22); only those who enjoy Him do not commit sin and are really free, living a life of liberty, release, and freedom from bondage (John 8:36):
A.　If we do not enjoy the Lord sufficiently, we will still be in bondage to many things; making up our mind will not work; we must continually come to the Lord to eat and enjoy Him—1 Cor. 1:9; Rev. 2:7; Isa. 55:1-2.
B.　We must be those who take the way of enjoying Christ as the tree of life in both our living and our service (John 6:57, 63; 2 Cor. 3:3-6; 1 John 5:16a); the tree of life in Genesis is the law of the Spirit of life in our spirit, and the tree of right and wrong is the law of sin and of death in our flesh (2:9; Rom. 8:2, 6).
C.　Only those who enjoy Christ as the law of the Spirit of life by setting their mind on the spirit do not practice sin and are really free; when we contact the Lord as the law of the Spirit of life in our spirit through the exercise of our spirit, we enjoy Christ as all the myriad and rich aspects of the jubilee—John 8:11-12, 24, 28, 31-36; Rom. 8:2, 6, 16; Phil. 1:19.
D.　Christ as the jubilee within us frees us from our poverty, captivity, blindness, and oppression— Eccl. 1:2, 14; 3:11; Phil. 3:8; 2 Pet. 2:22; Luke 12:21; Rev. 3:17.
E.　Paul was a person who "switched on" the law of the Spirit of life by serving God in his spirit out of his first love for the Lord—Rom. 1:9; 5:5; 8:35-39; Rev. 2:4-5:
1.　To love the Lord with the first love is to give Him the first place in all things and in all matters, regarding Him as everything in our life—Col. 1:18b, 10; 1 Cor. 2:9-10.
2.　When God comes into us and comes out of us, that is our service to Him; we work together with Christ in the churches, where we render our first love to Him—S. S. 7:12; 2 Cor. 6:1a; Phil. 3:3; Mark 12:30.
F.　God's salvation causes us to have real freedom; our possession is God, and our freedom comes from our enjoyment of God:
1.　If man does not enjoy God, he cannot have real freedom; freedom means release, to be freed from all bondage, all heavy burden, all oppression, and all enslavement—John 8:32, 36; Gal. 5:1; 2 Cor. 3:17:
a.　If a man does not have God, whatever he tries to enjoy apart from God is dog food, refuse, and dung—Phil. 3:7-9; cf. 2 Pet. 2:22.
b.　Satan is called Beelzebul, which means "the lord of the dunghill," from Beelzebub, meaning "the lord of flies"; Satan specializes in leading sinners like flies to feed on dung—Matt. 10:25; 12:24, 27; 2 Kings 1:2.
2.　Everything in our life can be a bondage to us, and we can be slaves under any matter; first, Satan captured us; then he came to dwell in us as the inciter, the instigator, of our sins; the result is that he became our illegal master, and we became his captives to the extent that we were unable to do good and could only commit sins—John 8:34; Rom. 7:14; 1 John 5:19.
G.　We have been conquered by Christ to be His captives, and our move in our ministry for Christ is a celebration of Christ's victory for His triumphant glory (2 Cor. 2:12-14); Christ rescued us from Satan's captivity (Psa. 68:18; Eph. 4:8); now that we belong to Him, He alone is our Teacher and Master (Matt. 23:8; Exo. 21:6), and we are "free indeed" (John 8:36; cf. 2 Cor. 10:3-5).
IV.　The living of the jubilee is a living in the enjoyment of Christ as the law of the Spirit of life, a living of enjoying God as our inheritance and real freedom:
A.　The only way to be released from the three kinds of labor in human life—the labor to be a good person, the labor of anxiety, and the labor of suffering—is to take Christ as our enjoyment, satisfaction, and rest—Rom. 7:24—8:2; Phil. 4:5-7; 2 Cor. 12:9.
B.　The Christian life should be a life full of enjoying the Lord, a life full of joy and praises; when we enjoy the Lord fully, He becomes our jubilee; the tone of an overcoming living is the tone of rejoicing, thanking, and praising God continually—1 Thes. 5:16-18; Psa. 50:14, 23; 106:12.
C.　The living of the jubilee is a life in which we take God Himself, Christ Himself, in every situation; then He becomes the primary factor and center in us to lead us and overrule all the troubles of human life—John 6:16-21; Col. 1:17b, 18b.
D.　Paul learned the secret of living in the jubilee, the secret of gaining Christ in any kind of environment (Phil. 3:8-9); because everything is under His sovereignty, we should pray, "Lord, fill me, gain me, and possess me; no matter what my outward situation is, I just want to enjoy You"—4:5-7, 11-13.
E.　We should all have one heart—to love God, to seek God, to live God, and to be constituted with God that we may be His expression—and one way—the Triune God Himself as the inner law of the Spirit of life with its divine capacity—Jer. 32:39.
V.　The experience and enjoyment of the law of the Spirit of life as the reality of the jubilee in Romans 8 is the reality of the Body of Christ—the corporate living of the perfected God-men—displayed in Romans 12 through 16; this reality consummates in the New Jerusalem:
A.　God accomplishes His economy by dispensing Himself into us as the law of the Spirit of life— 8:2, 6, 10-11; Rev. 22:1-2a.
B.　The law of the Spirit of life constitutes us to be the members of the Body of Christ, with all kinds of functions—Col. 2:19; Eph. 4:11, 16; Rom. 12:4-8.
C.　Through the spontaneous, automatic function of the law of the Spirit of life within us, we are enabled to know God, gain God, and thereby live God, causing us to be constituted with God that we may become His increase and His enlargement to be His fullness for His expression—Eph. 1:22-23; 3:19-21.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第十三篇　学习享受基督作生命之灵的律的秘诀，以活在新约禧年的实际里
Learning the Secret of Enjoying Christ as the Law of the Spirit of Life to Live in the Reality of the New Testament Jubilee
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
读经：利二五8～17，赛六一1～3，路四16～22，罗八2，16
壹　利未记二十五章八至十七节里的禧年，作为预言记载在以赛亚六十一章一至三节，实际的应验在路加四章十六至二十二节：─引用经文
I.　The year of jubilee in Leviticus 25:8-17 is recorded as a prophecy in Isaiah 61:1-3 and fulfilled in reality in Luke 4:16-22:
一　禧年有两项主要的福分，就是各人归回失去的产业，以及从奴役得着释放─利二五8～17：
A.　In the year of jubilee there were two main blessings: the returning of every man to his lost possession and the liberation from slavery—Lev. 25:8-17:
1　每一个卖了他所分得美地一分产业的，在禧年要归回自己的产业，而无须付赎价（10，13，28）；并且凡卖了自己作奴仆的，要重得自由，归回本家（39～41）。─引用经文
1.　In the year of jubilee everyone who had sold his possession, his allotted portion of the good land, was returned to it without paying anything to redeem it (vv. 10, 13, 28), and everyone who had sold himself into slavery regained his freedom and returned to his family (vv. 39-41).
2　归回自己的产业以及得自由归回本家，表征在新约的禧年里，信徒已经归回神，就是他们所失去神圣的产业，并且从一切捆绑得释放，回到召会，就是他们神圣的家─弗一13～14，约八32，36，参诗六八5～6。
2.　Returning to one's possession and being freed and returning to one's family signify that in the New Testament jubilee the believers have returned to God as their lost divine possession, have been released from all bondage, and have returned to the church as their divine family—Eph. 1:13-14; John 8:32, 36; cf. Psa. 68:5-6.
二　在旧约的预表里，禧年持续一年之久，其应验却是指整个新约时代，恩典时代，这是神悦纳归回的罪囚的时候（赛四九8，路十五17～24，林后六2），也是那些在罪的捆绑下受压制的人享受神救恩之释放的时候（罗七14～八2）。─引用经文
B.　In the Old Testament type the jubilee lasted for one year, but in the fulfillment it refers to the entire New Testament age, the age of grace, as the time when God accepts the returned captives of sin (Isa. 49:8; Luke 15:17-24; 2 Cor. 6:2) and when those oppressed under the bondage of sin enjoy the release of God's salvation (Rom. 7:14—8:2).
贰　新约时代就是狂喜时代，基督徒乃是狂喜的人；若是我们从来没有在神面前狂喜过，就表明我们对神的享受不够─林后六2，五13～15，徒十一5，二二17，诗四三4上，五一12，彼前一8，赛十二3～6：
II.　The New Testament age is an age of ecstasy, and a Christian is a person in ecstasy; if we have never been in ecstasy before God, this shows that we do not have a sufficient enjoyment of God—2 Cor. 6:2; 5:13-15; Acts 11:5; 22:17; Psa. 43:4a; 51:12; 1 Pet. 1:8; Isa. 12:3-6:
一　“禧年”的意思就是无忧无虑、无牵无挂、无缺无乏、无病无灾，什么难处都没有，什么都是好处；因此，一切应心，万事如意，逍遥自在，狂喜欢腾─腓四6～7，11～13，诗一〇三1～5。
A.　Jubilee means having no worry or anxiety, no concern or care, no lack or shortage, no sickness or calamity, and no problems whatsoever but, rather, having all benefits; hence, all things are pleas-ant and satisfying to our heart, and we are free from anxiety, at ease, excited, and exultant— Phil. 4:6-7, 11-13; Psa. 103:1-5.
二　我们必须接受主耶稣在我们里面作真正的禧年；我们得着了祂，就有神作我们的产业，并且能蒙拯救脱离罪和撒但的辖制，而有真正的自由与安息─徒二六18，弗一13～14，西一12，太十一28，约八32，36。
B.　We must receive the Lord Jesus as the real jubilee in us; if we have Him, we have God as our possession and can be delivered from the bondage of sin and Satan to have real freedom and rest—Acts 26:18; Eph. 1:13-14; Col. 1:12; Matt. 11:28; John 8:32, 36.
三　我们接受基督作我们的救主和生命时，祂就作为生命之灵的律进到我们里面作我们的禧年，但我们若没有让基督活在我们里面，也不凭基督活着，我们就还没有实际的活在禧年里─利二五11～12，罗八2：
C.　When we receive Christ as our Savior and life, He comes into us as the law of the Spirit of life to be our jubilee, but unless we allow Him to live in us and unless we live by Him, we are not practically living in the jubilee—Lev. 25:11-12; Rom. 8:2:
1　我们的心若放在主以外任何的人事物上，乃是拜偶像，结局都是苦恼─约壹五21，参结十四3，5，六9。
1.　If our heart is set on any person, thing, or matter other than the Lord, this is idolatry, and the end is wretchedness—1 John 5:21; cf. Ezek. 14:3, 5; 6:9.
2　我们若让基督活在我们里面，并凭祂活着，一切就都应心如意；否则一切就都是难处，凡事都没有禧年。
2.　If we allow Christ to live in us and we live by Him, everything is to our satisfaction; otherwise, everything is a problem, and nothing is a jubilee.
四　只有当这位包罗万有的基督给我们得着了，给我们享受了，我们才可能一切应心，万事如意；不是外面的人事物，乃是里面的基督，能叫我们安稳无忧的面对各样的环境─腓三8～9，四5～8，11～13：
D.　Everything can be satisfying to us only after we have gained the all-inclusive Christ as our enjoyment; it is not outward persons, matters, or things but Christ within us who enables us to be calm and free of worries as we face all kinds of situations—Phil. 3:8-9; 4:5-8, 11-13:
1　亚当没有接受生命树，就失去他享受神的分；世上一切不信的人都失去神作他们的产业和享受，并且将自己的肢体卖给罪，成为罪的奴仆─弗二12，罗七14，六19。
1.　Adam lost his portion of the enjoyment of God when he did not take the tree of life; all the unbelieving people of the world have lost God as their possession and enjoyment and have sold their members to sin in order to become slaves of sin—Eph. 2:12; Rom. 7:14; 6:19.
2　人生不过是劳苦愁烦，转眼成空；人生的实况乃是虚空的虚空，空中之空─都是捕风─诗九十10，七三14，16～17，25，传一2～11，14。
2.　Human life is nothing but labor and sorrow and will soon be gone; the true condition of human life is vanity of vanities, emptiness of emptinesses—a chasing after wind—Psa. 90:10; 73:14, 16-17, 25; Eccl. 1:2-11, 14.
五　信徒享受基督作恩典的禧年，要带进千年国里对禧年完满的享受，以及在新天新地新耶路撒冷里最完满的享受─腓三14，启二二1～2上。
E.　The believers' enjoyment of Christ as the jubilee of grace will issue in the full enjoyment of the jubilee in the millennium and in the fullest enjoyment in the New Jerusalem in the new heaven and new earth—Phil. 3:14; Rev. 22:1-2a.
六　利未记二十五章十节的“禧年”这辞，意思是“呼喊的时候”，或“吹公羊角的时候”；我们传福音就是吹公羊角，向世人宣扬：“看哪，现在正是最可蒙悦纳的时候；看哪，现在正是拯救的日子”─林后六2，赛六一1～3：
F.　The word jubilee in Leviticus 25:10 means "a time of shouting," or "a time of the trumpeting of the ram's horn"; our preaching of the gospel is our blowing of the trumpet to proclaim to the world, "Behold, now is the well-acceptable time; behold, now is the day of salvation"—2 Cor. 6:2; Isa. 61:1-3:
1　神造人时，定意要将自己在基督里给人，作人的产业，人的基业（创二9，十三12～15，诗十六5，九十1）；然而，人堕落了，在堕落中人失去神作为产业（创三24，四16，弗二12），将自己卖给罪、撒但和世界，受其奴役（约八34，罗七14下，加四8，多三3，约壹五19下）。─引用经文
1.　When God created man, He intended to give Himself in Christ to man as man's possession, man's inheritance (Gen. 2:9; 13:12-15; Psa. 16:5; 90:1); however, man became fallen, and in the fall man lost God as his possession (Gen. 3:24; 4:16; Eph. 2:12) and sold himself into slavery under sin, Satan, and the world (John 8:34; Rom. 7:14b; Gal. 4:8; Titus 3:3; 1 John 5:19b).
2　堕落的人没有真实的住处；他们都是漂泊、流浪、无家可归的，因为神是人真正的居所─诗九十1，创二八17～19，约十五4，太十一28。
2.　Fallen people have no real dwelling place; they are drifting about and wandering without a home, because God is man's real dwelling place—Psa. 90:1; Gen. 28:17-19; John 15:4; Matt. 11:28.
3　神新约的救恩乃是将堕落的人带回归神，作他神圣的产业（加三14，弗一14，西一12，路十五12～24），释放人脱离罪、撒但和世界的奴役（约八32，罗六6，14，八2，来二14～15，约十二31），并将人恢复到他神圣的家庭，就是神的家里（加六10，弗二19），使他享受神恩典里的交通（林后十三14）。─引用经文
3.　God's New Testament salvation brings fallen man back to God as his divine possession (Gal. 3:14; Eph. 1:14; Col. 1:12; Luke 15:12-24), releases man from slavery under sin, Satan, and the world (John 8:32; Rom. 6:6, 14; 8:2; Heb. 2:14-15; John 12:31), and restores man to his divine family, the household of God (Gal. 6:10; Eph. 2:19), that he may enjoy fellowship in God's grace (2 Cor. 13:14).
叁　我们惟有享受基督作生命之灵的律，才能得着释放，才有真自由，使我们活在新约禧年的实际里（罗八2，路四16～22）；惟有享受祂的人能不犯罪，而有真自由，过一个自由、释放、脱离辖制的生活─约八36：
III.　We can be released and have real freedom only by enjoying Christ as the law of the Spirit of life so that we may live in the reality of the New Testament jubilee (Rom. 8:2; Luke 4:16-22); only those who enjoy Him do not commit sin and are really free, living a life of liberty, release, and freedom from bondage (John 8:36):
一　如果我们享受主不够，就在许多事上还会受捆绑；立志没有用，我们一定要不断的来到主这里，吃祂并享受祂─林前一9，启二7，赛五五1～2。
A.　If we do not enjoy the Lord sufficiently, we will still be in bondage to many things; making up our mind will not work; we must continually come to the Lord to eat and enjoy Him—1 Cor. 1:9; Rev. 2:7; Isa. 55:1-2.
二　在我们的生活和事奉上，我们必须是走享受基督作生命树的路的人（约六57，63，林后三3～6，约壹五16上）；创世记里的生命树，是我们灵里生命之灵的律，善恶树是我们肉体里罪与死的律（二9，罗八2，6）。─引用经文
B.　We must be those who take the way of enjoying Christ as the tree of life in both our living and our service (John 6:57, 63; 2 Cor. 3:3-6; 1 John 5:16a); the tree of life in Genesis is the law of the Spirit of life in our spirit, and the tree of right and wrong is the law of sin and of death in our flesh (2:9; Rom. 8:2, 6).
三　惟有借着将心思置于灵，享受基督作生命之灵的律的人才不实行罪，才有真自由；我们借着操练灵接触那在我们灵里的主作为生命之灵的律时，就享受基督作禧年无数丰富的方面─约八11～12，24，28，31～36，罗八2，6，16，腓一19。
C.　Only those who enjoy Christ as the law of the Spirit of life by setting their mind on the spirit do not practice sin and are really free; when we contact the Lord as the law of the Spirit of life in our spirit through the exercise of our spirit, we enjoy Christ as all the myriad and rich aspects of the jubilee—John 8:11-12, 24, 28, 31-36; Rom. 8:2, 6, 16; Phil. 1:19.
四　基督在我们里面作禧年，释放我们脱离贫穷、被掳、瞎眼和受压制─传一2，14，三11，腓三8，彼后二22，路十二21，启三17。
D.　Christ as the jubilee within us frees us from our poverty, captivity, blindness, and oppression— Eccl. 1:2, 14; 3:11; Phil. 3:8; 2 Pet. 2:22; Luke 12:21; Rev. 3:17.
五　保罗是“打开”生命之灵的律“开关”的人；他打开这开关乃是借着在他的灵里，出于他对主起初的爱事奉神─罗一9，五5，八35～39，启二4～5：
E.　Paul was a person who "switched on" the law of the Spirit of life by serving God in his spirit out of his first love for the Lord—Rom. 1:9; 5:5; 8:35-39; Rev. 2:4-5:
1　用起初的爱爱主，就是在一切事物上让祂居首位，尊重祂是我们生活中的一切─西一18下，10，林前二9～10。
1.　To love the Lord with the first love is to give Him the first place in all things and in all matters, regarding Him as everything in our life—Col. 1:18b, 10; 1 Cor. 2:9-10.
2　在我们身上，神进来了，神再出去，那就是我们对祂的事奉；我们乃是在众召会中与基督同工，在那里将我们起初的爱给祂─歌七12，林后六1上，腓三3，可十二30。
2.　When God comes into us and comes out of us, that is our service to Him; we work together with Christ in the churches, where we render our first love to Him—S. S. 7:12; 2 Cor. 6:1a; Phil. 3:3; Mark 12:30.
六　神的救恩使我们有真自由；我们的产业是神，我们的自由来自我们对神的享受：
F.　God's salvation causes us to have real freedom; our possession is God, and our freedom comes from our enjoyment of God:
1　人若不享受神，是不会有真自由的；自由就是释放，就是脱开一切捆绑、一切重担、一切压制、和一切辖制─约八32，36，加五1，林后三17：
1.　If man does not enjoy God, he cannot have real freedom; freedom means release, to be freed from all bondage, all heavy burden, all oppression, and all enslavement—John 8:32, 36; Gal. 5:1; 2 Cor. 3:17:
a　人若没有神，那么他在神以外所尝试享受的一切都是狗食、废物、粪土─腓三7～9，参彼后二22。
a.　If a man does not have God, whatever he tries to enjoy apart from God is dog food, refuse, and dung—Phil. 3:7-9; cf. 2 Pet. 2:22.
b　撒但称为别西布尔（Beelzebul），意“粪堆之王”；这名源自“别西卜”（Be?elzebub），意“苍蝇之王”；撒但专门带着罪人像苍蝇一样吃粪─太十25，十二24，27，王下一2。
b.　Satan is called Beelzebul, which means "the lord of the dunghill," from Beelzebub, meaning "the lord of flies"; Satan specializes in leading sinners like flies to feed on dung—Matt. 10:25; 12:24, 27; 2 Kings 1:2.
2　我们人生里的每一件事，都可能是我们的辖制；在每一件事之下我们都可能作奴隶；首先撒但把我们俘掳了，然后他就来住在我们里面，作我们犯罪的主动者、主使者；结果他就成了我们非法的主人，我们就作了他的俘虏，使我们好事不作，专作犯罪的事─约八34，罗七14，约壹五19。
2.　Everything in our life can be a bondage to us, and we can be slaves under any matter; first, Satan captured us; then he came to dwell in us as the inciter, the instigator, of our sins; the result is that he became our illegal master, and we became his captives to the extent that we were unable to do good and could only commit sins—John 8:34; Rom. 7:14; 1 John 5:19.
七　我们已经被基督征服，成了祂的俘虏，我们在我们的职事里为着基督的行动，乃是庆祝基督的得胜，使祂得着凯旋的荣耀（林后二12～14）；基督拯救我们脱离撒但的掳掠（诗六八18，弗四8）；现今我们既属于祂，惟有祂是我们的夫子与主人（太二三8，出二一6），我们乃是“真自由了”（约八36，参林后十3～5）。─引用经文
G.　We have been conquered by Christ to be His captives, and our move in our ministry for Christ is a celebration of Christ's victory for His triumphant glory (2 Cor. 2:12-14); Christ rescued us from Satan's captivity (Psa. 68:18; Eph. 4:8); now that we belong to Him, He alone is our Teacher and Master (Matt. 23:8; Exo. 21:6), and we are "free indeed" (John 8:36; cf. 2 Cor. 10:3-5).
肆　禧年的生活乃是享受基督作生命之灵的律的生活，就是享受神作我们的基业和真自由的生活：
IV.　The living of the jubilee is a living in the enjoyment of Christ as the law of the Spirit of life, a living of enjoying God as our inheritance and real freedom:
一　得释放脱离人生的三种劳苦─作好人的劳苦、挂虑的劳苦、和受苦的劳苦─惟一的路，是以基督作我们的享受、满足和安息─罗七24～八2，腓四5～7，林后十二9。
A.　The only way to be released from the three kinds of labor in human life—the labor to be a good person, the labor of anxiety, and the labor of suffering—is to take Christ as our enjoyment, satisfaction, and rest—Rom. 7:24—8:2; Phil. 4:5-7; 2 Cor. 12:9.
二　基督徒的生活应该是满了享受主的生活，满了喜乐和赞美的生活；当我们完满享受主时，祂就成了我们的禧年；得胜生活的腔调乃是一直喜乐并感谢赞美神的腔调─帖前五16～18，诗五十14，23，一〇六12。
B.　The Christian life should be a life full of enjoying the Lord, a life full of joy and praises; when we enjoy the Lord fully, He becomes our jubilee; the tone of an overcoming living is the tone of rejoicing, thanking, and praising God continually—1 Thes. 5:16-18; Psa. 50:14, 23; 106:12.
三　禧年的生活，就是我们在任何情况中都取用神自己，取用基督自己的生活；然后祂就在我们里面作主因、作中心，带领我们克服人生一切的困扰─约六16～21，西一17下，18下。
C.　The living of the jubilee is a life in which we take God Himself, Christ Himself, in every situation; then He becomes the primary factor and center in us to lead us and overrule all the troubles of human life—John 6:16-21; Col. 1:17b, 18b.
四　保罗学得活在禧年里的秘诀，就是在各种的环境里赢得基督（腓三8～9）；因着一切都在祂的主宰之下，所以我们应该祷告说，“主阿，求你充满我，得着我，占有我；不管外面情况如何，我就是要享受你”─四5～7，11～13。
D.　Paul learned the secret of living in the jubilee, the secret of gaining Christ in any kind of environment (Phil. 3:8-9); because everything is under His sovereignty, we should pray, "Lord, fill me, gain me, and possess me; no matter what my outward situation is, I just want to enjoy You"—4:5-7, 11-13.
五　我们都该有一个心─爱神、寻求神、活神、并被神构成，使我们成为祂的彰显；我们也该有一条路─三一神自己作为内里生命之灵的律连同其神圣的性能─耶三二39。
E.　We should all have one heart—to love God, to seek God, to live God, and to be constituted with God that we may be His expression—and one way—the Triune God Himself as the inner law of the Spirit of life with its divine capacity—Jer. 32:39.
伍　在罗马八章里经历并享受生命之灵的律作禧年的实际，乃是十二至十六章所展示之基督身体─得成全之神人的团体生活─的实际；这实际终极完成于新耶路撒冷：
V.　The experience and enjoyment of the law of the Spirit of life as the reality of the jubilee in Romans 8 is the reality of the Body of Christ—the corporate living of the perfected God-men—displayed in Romans 12 through 16; this reality consummates in the New Jerusalem:
一　神完成祂的经纶，是借着将祂自己分赐到我们里面作生命之灵的律─八2，6，10～11，启二二1～2上。
A.　God accomplishes His economy by dispensing Himself into us as the law of the Spirit of life— 8:2, 6, 10-11; Rev. 22:1-2a.
二　生命之灵的律将我们构成基督身体具有各种功用的肢体─西二19，弗四11，16，罗十二4～8。
B.　The law of the Spirit of life constitutes us to be the members of the Body of Christ, with all kinds of functions—Col. 2:19; Eph. 4:11, 16; Rom. 12:4-8.
三　借着我们里面生命之灵的律自发自动的功用，我们就能认识神、得着神、因而把神活出来，使我们被神构成，得以成为祂的扩增和扩大，作祂的丰满，使祂得着彰显─弗一22～23，三19～21。
C.　Through the spontaneous, automatic function of the law of the Spirit of life within us, we are enabled to know God, gain God, and thereby live God, causing us to be constituted with God that we may become His increase and His enlargement to be His fullness for His expression—Eph. 1:22-23; 3:19-21.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
第十四篇　活在生命之灵的律作为爱的律法里，以成就我们模成神长子形像的定命
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
读经：罗八2，28～29，加六2～3，约十三34，约壹四16～21，林前八1，十三4～8上，13
壹　神的经纶就是祂的心意，要将自己作到我们里面，使祂自己成为人，好使人在生命和性情上成为神，但无分于神格，好使祂“人化”了，而我们“神化”了，为着建造召会作基督生机的身体，以终极完成新耶路撒冷：
一　基督徒的生活乃是基督自己借著作为生命之灵的律运行在我们里面，而从我们活出来─诗歌三〇四首，罗八2。
二　每当我们觉得自己软弱、低沉、退后时，我们去祷告、亲近主，里面生命之灵的律立刻自动自发的运行，使我们得着复苏─诗六二8，耶十七7～8，诗八十1，3，7，18～19。
三　内住的生命之灵的律乃是盖印的灵，对我们就是一只“订婚戒指”，向所有人指明，我们已经许配给基督，我们属于基督，并为基督占有─林后十一2，路十五22，弗一13，四30。
四　三一神经过过程并终极完成为生命之灵的律，就是赐生命的灵，赐人生命的那灵；如今祂在我们里面作为自动的原则和自发的能力，将祂自己作为生命（原文，“奏厄”）分赐到我们整个三部分的人里─约六63，十四6上，十10下，罗八2，10，6，11。
贰　“万有都互相效力，叫爱神的人得益处，就是按祂旨意被召的人。因为神所预知的人，祂也预定他们模成神儿子的形像，使祂儿子在许多弟兄中作长子”─28～29节：
一　罗马八章论到包罗万有的灵赐生命给我们这人的三部分，目标是为将我们模成神长子的形像；包罗万有之灵独一的功用乃是将奏厄，就是神圣的生命，分授到我们里面─林后三6：
1　长子是原型，是标准的模型，为着大量复制出神许多的儿子，就是长子许多的弟兄，构成祂的身体，作神团体的彰显─罗八29，弗四20～21。
2　神大量复制这原型的作法，乃是将祂活的原型，就是长子，作到我们全人里面；我们若与这奇妙的原型合作，向祂敞开，祂就要从我们的灵向外扩展到我们心的各部分里─三16～21。
二　那灵安排我们的环境，使万人、万事与万物都互相效力，叫我们得益处；罗马八章二十八节的“益处”，乃指更多得着基督作到我们里面；生命之灵的律用生命供应我们，以变化我们并将我们模成神长子基督的形像，使我们成为献给神的基督馨香之气─耶四八11，林后二15，歌四16。
三　我们模成神长子的形像，乃是我们的定命，也是神圣生命在我们里面作工的目标；我们照着那在耶稣身上是实际者学了基督，就是在基督这榜样的模子里，模成基督的形像，在复活里接受祂作我们神圣的生命，而在神里面、同着神、为着神、凭着神、并向着神作一切，使神得着荣耀─罗八29，弗一4～5，四20～21，罗十一36。
四　我们被模成，乃是我们在神圣生命上的成熟，借此我们完满的有分于神的神性，而在具有祂的神圣成分并经历祂生机的救恩上，得到具体：
1　变化是我们在天然的生命里新陈代谢的改变，成熟乃是我们被那改变我们的神圣生命所充满─林后三18，来六1上，西一28～29。
2　生命成熟是被作生命的神所充满，祝福乃是生命的满溢，就是神借着人生命成熟而有的满溢；祝福别人就是将人带到神面前，并将人带进神圣三一的神圣分赐里─民六22～27，林后十三14，彼前三8～9。
五　包罗万有、赐生命、内住的生命之灵的律，正将积极而有能的神圣生命注入我们里面，在我们里面作工，要“基督化”我们，使我们在生命、性情和彰显上，与基督一模一样。
六　我们可以借着神圣生命的显出，看出人是否享受并经历奏厄，就是神圣的生命─参民六6～9：
1　那些不肯完全向主敞开、接受祂作生命的光的人，虽然还能用头脑听信息并读圣经，但他们所听的，所读的，不过成了他们定罪别人的张本，批评别人的工具，而自己却一点光都得不着。
2　那些向主关闭的人，专会定罪人，批评人，对别人的光景看得很清楚，而对自己的情形却一点不认识；这证明他们完全是在黑暗里！
3　我们在聚会中是如何听一篇健康、正确的信息，就可以显明在我们的心思里是生命或死亡；我们若喜乐的接受信息，就显明心思里满有生命；然而，我们里面若对信息起怀疑或争论，就显明我们心思里的死亡；听众心思里的生命或死亡，可以供应或杀死讲者的灵。
4　我们若满了生命，尽管我们也许没有作什么，但我们这人就会彰显生命，并供应生命给周围的人─约壹五16上。
叁　生命之灵的律乃是基督的律法作为爱的律法─罗八2，加六2，约十三34：
一　神先爱我们，将祂的爱注入我们里面，并且在我们里面产生出爱来，使我们能用这爱爱祂，并爱众弟兄─约壹四19～21。
二　保罗在林前十三章所描述的爱，乃是神圣生命的彰显（4～8上）；不仅如此，爱乃是那灵的果子，这事实指明爱的本质必须是那灵（加五22）；我们若没有爱，我们的说话就如同鸣的锣、响的钹，发出声音却没有生命（林前十三1）。─引用经文
三　爱是不嫉妒，不轻易发怒，不计算人的恶，凡事包容，凡事忍耐，比一切存留得更长久，并且是最大的─4～8上，13节。
四　爱的律法必须由生命之灵的律将其实化，使我们能彼此担当重担，成为我们在灵里并凭着灵而行的自然结果（加六2，五16，25）；但我们若满了骄傲，就不能担当别人的重担；这是因为我们自己欺骗自己，自以为是什么，其实我们什么也不是（六3）。─引用经文
五　当爱的律法在我们里面得以发动，我们就自动并自然的成为牧人，有我们父神爱和赦免的心，并我们救主基督牧养和寻找的灵，寻找并找着失去的那只羊─约二一15～17，路十五1～7。
六　当爱的律法在我们里面得以发动，我们在主里的劳苦就是爱心的劳苦（林前十五58，帖前一3～4）；在其中我们“扶助软弱的人”（徒二十35）并“扶持软弱的人”（帖前五14）；“软弱的人”指那些在灵、魂、体方面软弱，或是在信心上软弱的人（罗十四1，十五1）。─引用经文
七　我们从神所接受的生命乃是爱的生命；基督曾在这世上活出神就是爱的生活，如今祂是我们的生命，使我们能在这世上活出同样爱的生活，与祂所是的一样─约壹三14，五1，二6，四17。
八　我们必须是一个被基督的爱冲没并冲激的人；神圣的爱该像大水澎湃冲向我们，迫使我们情不自禁的向祂活着─林后五14。
九　弟兄相爱是旧诫命，也是新诫命：是旧诫命，乃因信徒从基督徒生活的开始就有了；是新诫命，乃因在基督徒的行事为人上，这诫命一再露出新的曙光，一再以新的亮光及新鲜的能力照耀─约壹二7～8，三11，23，参约十三34。
十　召会生活乃是弟兄相爱的生活（约壹四7～8，约贰5～6，约十五12，17，启三7，弗五2，参犹12上），并且身体在爱里把自己建造起来（弗四16）。─引用经文
十一　神赐给我们的灵，就是蒙了重生的灵，乃是爱的灵；我们需要有一个火热的爱的灵，以征服今日召会的堕落─提后一6～7，罗十二11。
十二　“知识是叫人自高自大，惟有爱建造人”；我们可能听了职事的信息，只得了一些知识，就自高自大（林前八1下，参林后三6）；彼此相爱是我们属于基督的表记（约十三34～35）。─引用经文
十三　在召会中间好为首，乃与爱众弟兄相对─约叁9：
1　在主工作中的争竞，不仅是雄心的表记，也是骄傲的表记；题到自己的才能、成功、完全和美德，乃是骄傲的一种轻率形态。
2　看自己过于所当看的，是骄傲的另一种形态（罗十二3）；自夸、自高、自荣、食图虚荣，都是骄傲丑陋、卑下的表现（加五25～26）。─引用经文
十四　正如主耶稣舍了祂的魂生命，使我们能得着神圣的生命，我们在实行身体的生活时，也需要舍去我们的魂生命并否认己，以爱弟兄并将生命供应给他们─约壹三16，约十11，17～18，十五13，弗四15～16，29～五2，林后三6，四12～13，十二15，罗十二9～13。
十五　我们需要丧失我们的魂生命，不爱这世界及其享乐；反之，我们应当接受并彰显是爱的神，以此为我们的喜乐、娱乐、消遣和快乐─约壹二15～17，太十六25～26，诗三六8～9，参提后三1～5。
十六　在召会生活中，弟兄相爱乃是实际的表现在顾到缺乏圣徒的需要，而没有任何自私的目的或外表自我的显扬；在与缺乏圣徒分享物质的东西时，主生命的恩典连同祂的爱，就在基督身体的众肢体之间涌流，并注入他们里面─约壹三17～18，太六1～4，罗十二13，林后八1～7。
十七　我们住在爱里面，习惯的用神的爱爱人，就履行了我们怀着雄心大志，要讨主的喜悦，并且不会惧怕主再来时会受祂刑罚─约壹四16～18，林后五9～11，太二五21。
十八　为着建造召会作基督生机的身体，在我们的所是和所作上，爱乃是极超越的路─林前十二31下～十三8上。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
CHAPTERS FIVE THROUGH EIGHT OF ROMANS— THE KERNEL OF THE BIBLE
Message Fourteen
Living in the Law of the Spirit of Life as the Law of Love to Fulfill Our Destiny of Being Conformed to the Image of the Firstborn Son of God
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
Scripture Reading: Rom. 8:2, 28-29; Gal. 6:2-3; John 13:34; 1 John 4:16-21; 1 Cor. 8:1; 13:4-8a, 13
I.　God's economy is His intention to work Himself into us by making Himself man in order to make man God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead so that He is "man-ized" and we are "God-ized" for the building up of the church as the organic Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem:
A.　The Christian life is a life that is Christ Himself lived through us by His operating in us as the law of the Spirit of life—Hymns, #403; Rom. 8:2.
B.　Whenever we feel that we are weak, depressed, and backsliding, we can pray and draw near to the Lord, and spontaneously and automatically, the law of the Spirit of life will operate within us to revive us—Psa. 62:8; Jer. 17:7-8; Psa. 80:1, 3, 7, 18-19.
C.　The indwelling law of the Spirit of life is the sealing Spirit as an "engagement ring" to us, indicating to everyone that we are betrothed to Christ, that we belong to Christ, and that we are occupied by Christ—2 Cor. 11:2; Luke 15:22; Eph. 1:13; 4:30.
D.　The Triune God was processed and consummated to be the law of the Spirit of life as the life-giving Spirit, "the Spirit who gives life"; He is now within us as an automatic principle and spontaneous power to give Himself as life (Gk. zoe) to our entire tripartite being—John 6:63; 14:6a; 10:10b; Rom. 8:2, 10, 6, 11.
II.　"All things work together for good to those who love God, to those who are called according to His purpose. Because those whom He foreknew, He also predestinated to be conformed to the image of His Son, that He might be the Firstborn among many brothers"—vv. 28-29:
A.　Romans 8 concerns the all-inclusive Spirit giving life to the three parts of our being for the goal of conforming us to the image of the firstborn Son of God; the sole function of the all-inclusive Spirit is to impart zoe, the divine life, into us—2 Cor. 3:6:
1.　The firstborn Son is the prototype, the standard model, for the mass reproduction of the many sons of God, who are His many brothers to constitute His Body for God's corporate expression—Rom. 8:29; Eph. 4:20-21.
2.　God's way to mass reproduce this prototype is to work His living prototype, the first-born Son, into our entire being; if we cooperate with and open up to this wonderful prototype, He will spread outward from our spirit into all the parts of our heart— 3:16-21.
B.　The Spirit arranges our circumstances, causing all persons, all matters, and all things to work together for good; the "good" in Romans 8:28 refers to our gaining more of Christ, to our having Him wrought into our being; the law of the Spirit of life supplies us with life to transform us and to conform us to the image of Christ as the firstborn Son of God, making us a fragrance of Christ to God—Jer. 48:11; 2 Cor. 2:15; S. S. 4:16.
C.　For us to be conformed to the image of God's firstborn Son is our destiny and the goal of the working of the divine life within us; our learning Christ as the reality is in Jesus is to be molded into the pattern of Christ, conformed to the image of Christ, by taking Him as our divine life in resurrection to do everything in God, with God, for God, by God, and to God for the glory of God—Rom. 8:29; Eph. 1:4-5; 4:20-21; Rom. 11:36.
D.　Our conformation is our maturity in the divine life through which we participate in God's divinity in full and are solidified in the possession of His divine element and in the experience of His organic salvation:
1.　To be transformed is to be metabolically changed in our natural life; to be mature is to be filled with the divine life that changes us—2 Cor. 3:18; Heb. 6:1a; Col. 1:28-29.
2.　Maturity in life is a matter of being filled with God as life, and blessing is the over-flow of life, the overflow of God through the maturity in life; to bless others is to bring them into the presence of God and into the divine dispensing of the Divine Trinity—Num. 6:22-27; 2 Cor. 13:14; 1 Pet. 3:8-9.
E.　The all-inclusive, life-giving, indwelling law of the Spirit of life is infusing us with the active and energetic divine life, working within us to "Christify" us, to make us exactly the same as Christ in life, nature, and expression.
F.　We can see whether someone is enjoying and experiencing zoe, the divine life, by the manifestations of the divine life—cf. Num. 6:6-9:
1.　Those who are not willing to fully open themselves to the Lord to receive Him as the light of life may still use their mind to listen to messages and read the Bible, but what they hear and read become only a reference for them to judge others, an instrument to criticize others, while they themselves receive not a bit of light.
2.　Those who close themselves to the Lord are experts in judging and criticizing others; they are very clear about others' condition, but they do not know a bit concerning their own condition; this proves that they are entirely in darkness!
3.　The way that we listen to a healthy, proper message in a meeting may be a manifestation of life or death in our mind; if we receive the message with joy, this is the manifestation of a mind full of life; however, if we inwardly question and argue with the message, this is a manifestation of death in our mind; the life or death in the minds of the listeners can supply or kill the spirit of the speaking one.
4.　When we are full of life, although we may not do anything, our being will express life and minister life to those around us—1 John 5:16a.
III.　The law of the Spirit of life is the law of Christ as the law of love—Rom. 8:2; Gal. 6:2; John 13:34:
A.　God first loved us in that He infused us with His love and generated within us the love with which we love Him and the brothers—1 John 4:19-21.
B.　The love described by Paul in 1 Corinthians 13 is the expression of the divine life (vv. 4-8a); furthermore, the fact that love is the fruit of the Spirit indicates that the substance of love must be the Spirit (Gal. 5:22); if we do not have love, our speaking is like that of sounding brass and a clanging cymbal, which give sounds without life (1 Cor. 13:1).
C.　Love is not jealous, is not provoked, does not take account of evil, covers all things, endures all things, survives everything, and is the greatest—vv. 4-8a, 13.
D.　The law of love must be substantiated by the law of the Spirit of life so that we may be able to bear one another's burdens as a spontaneous result of our walking in and by the Spirit (Gal. 6:2; 5:16, 25), but if we are filled with pride, we will be unable to bear others' burdens; this is because we deceive ourselves by thinking that we are something when we are nothing (6:3).
E.　When the law of love is activated within us, we automatically and spontaneously will be shepherds who have the loving and forgiving heart of our Father God and the shepherding and seeking spirit of our Savior Christ, going after and finding the one sheep that is lost—John 21:15-17; Luke 15:1-7.
F.　When the law of love is activated within us, our labor in the Lord is a labor of love (1 Cor. 15:58; 1 Thes. 1:3-4) in which we "support the weak" (Acts 20:35) and "sustain the weak" (1 Thes. 5:14); the weak refers to those who are weak either in spirit or soul or body or who are weak in faith (Rom. 14:1; 15:1).
G.　The life that we have received from God is a life of love; Christ lived in this world a life of God as love, and He is now our life so that we may live the same life of love in this world and be the same as He is—1 John 3:14; 5:1; 2:6; 4:17.
H.　We must be persons who are flooded with and carried away by the love of Christ; the divine love should be like the rushing tide of great waters toward us, impelling us to live to Him beyond our own control—2 Cor. 5:14.
I.　The commandment regarding brotherly love is both old and new: old, because the believers have had it from the beginning of their Christian life; new, because in their Christian walk it dawns with new light and shines with new enlightenment and fresh power again and again—1 John 2:7-8; 3:11, 23; cf. John 13:34.
J.　The church life is a life of brotherly love (1 John 4:7-8; 2 John 5-6; John 15:12, 17; Rev. 3:7; Eph. 5:2; cf. Jude 12a), and the Body builds itself up in love (Eph. 4:16).
K.　Our God-given, regenerated spirit is a spirit of love; we need a burning spirit of love to conquer the degradation of today's church—2 Tim. 1:6-7; Rom. 12:11.
L.　"Knowledge puffs up, but love builds up"; we may listen to the messages of the ministry and become puffed up with mere knowledge (1 Cor. 8:1b; cf. 2 Cor. 3:6); loving one another is a sign that we belong to Christ (John 13:34-35).
M.　Loving to be first in the church is versus loving all the brothers—3 John 9:
1.　Rivalry in the Lord's work is not only a sign of ambition but also a sign of pride; referring to our capacity, success, perfection, and virtue is a careless form of pride.
2.　Thinking more highly of ourselves than we ought to think is another form of pride (Rom. 12:3); self-boasting, self-exaltation, self-glorification, and lusting after vainglory are all ugly and base expressions of pride (Gal. 5:25-26).
N.　Just as the Lord Jesus laid down His soul-life so that we might have the divine life, we need to lose our soul-life and deny the self to love the brothers and minister life to them in the practice of the Body life—1 John 3:16; John 10:11, 17-18; 15:13; Eph. 4:15-16, 29—5:2; 2 Cor. 3:6; 4:12-13; 12:15; Rom. 12:9-13.
O.　We need to lose our soul-life by not loving the world with its pleasure; instead, taking in God and expressing God as love should be our joy, amusement, entertainment, and happiness—1 John 2:15-17; Matt. 16:25-26; Psa. 36:8-9; cf. 2 Tim. 3:1-5.
P.　Brotherly love in the church life is expressed practically in our caring for the necessities of the needy saints without any self-serving purpose or outward self-display; in the sharing of material things with the needy saints, the grace of the Lord's life with His love flows among the members of the Body of Christ and is infused into them— 1 John 3:17-18; Matt. 6:1-4; Rom. 12:13; 2 Cor. 8:1-7.
Q.　Our abiding in love by habitually loving others with the love of God fulfills our determination to gain the honor of being well pleasing to Him and has no fear of being punished by the Lord at His coming back—1 John 4:16-18; 2 Cor. 5:9-11; Matt. 25:21.
R.　Love is the most excellent way for us to be anything or do anything for the building up of the church as the organic Body of Christ—1 Cor. 12:31b—13:8a.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第十四篇　活在生命之灵的律作为爱的律法里，以成就我们模成神长子形像的定命
Living in the Law of the Spirit of Life as the Law of Love to Fulfill Our Destiny of Being Conformed to the Image of the Firstborn Son of God
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
读经：罗八2，28～29，加六2～3，约十三34，约壹四16～21，林前八1，十三4～8上，13
壹　神的经纶就是祂的心意，要将自己作到我们里面，使祂自己成为人，好使人在生命和性情上成为神，但无分于神格，好使祂“人化”了，而我们“神化”了，为着建造召会作基督生机的身体，以终极完成新耶路撒冷：
I.　God's economy is His intention to work Himself into us by making Himself man in order to make man God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead so that He is "man-ized" and we are "God-ized" for the building up of the church as the organic Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem:
一　基督徒的生活乃是基督自己借著作为生命之灵的律运行在我们里面，而从我们活出来─诗歌三〇四首，罗八2。
A.　The Christian life is a life that is Christ Himself lived through us by His operating in us as the law of the Spirit of life—Hymns, #403; Rom. 8:2.
二　每当我们觉得自己软弱、低沉、退后时，我们去祷告、亲近主，里面生命之灵的律立刻自动自发的运行，使我们得着复苏─诗六二8，耶十七7～8，诗八十1，3，7，18～19。
B.　Whenever we feel that we are weak, depressed, and backsliding, we can pray and draw near to the Lord, and spontaneously and automatically, the law of the Spirit of life will operate within us to revive us—Psa. 62:8; Jer. 17:7-8; Psa. 80:1, 3, 7, 18-19.
三　内住的生命之灵的律乃是盖印的灵，对我们就是一只“订婚戒指”，向所有人指明，我们已经许配给基督，我们属于基督，并为基督占有─林后十一2，路十五22，弗一13，四30。
C.　The indwelling law of the Spirit of life is the sealing Spirit as an "engagement ring" to us, indicating to everyone that we are betrothed to Christ, that we belong to Christ, and that we are occupied by Christ—2 Cor. 11:2; Luke 15:22; Eph. 1:13; 4:30.
四　三一神经过过程并终极完成为生命之灵的律，就是赐生命的灵，赐人生命的那灵；如今祂在我们里面作为自动的原则和自发的能力，将祂自己作为生命（原文，“奏厄”）分赐到我们整个三部分的人里─约六63，十四6上，十10下，罗八2，10，6，11。
D.　The Triune God was processed and consummated to be the law of the Spirit of life as the life-giving Spirit, "the Spirit who gives life"; He is now within us as an automatic principle and spontaneous power to give Himself as life (Gk. zoe) to our entire tripartite being—John 6:63; 14:6a; 10:10b; Rom. 8:2, 10, 6, 11.
贰　“万有都互相效力，叫爱神的人得益处，就是按祂旨意被召的人。因为神所预知的人，祂也预定他们模成神儿子的形像，使祂儿子在许多弟兄中作长子”─28～29节：
II.　"All things work together for good to those who love God, to those who are called according to His purpose. Because those whom He foreknew, He also predestinated to be conformed to the image of His Son, that He might be the Firstborn among many brothers"—vv. 28-29:
一　罗马八章论到包罗万有的灵赐生命给我们这人的三部分，目标是为将我们模成神长子的形像；包罗万有之灵独一的功用乃是将奏厄，就是神圣的生命，分授到我们里面─林后三6：
A.　Romans 8 concerns the all-inclusive Spirit giving life to the three parts of our being for the goal of conforming us to the image of the firstborn Son of God; the sole function of the all-inclusive Spirit is to impart zoe, the divine life, into us—2 Cor. 3:6:
1　长子是原型，是标准的模型，为着大量复制出神许多的儿子，就是长子许多的弟兄，构成祂的身体，作神团体的彰显─罗八29，弗四20～21。
1.　The firstborn Son is the prototype, the standard model, for the mass reproduction of the many sons of God, who are His many brothers to constitute His Body for God's corporate expression—Rom. 8:29; Eph. 4:20-21.
2　神大量复制这原型的作法，乃是将祂活的原型，就是长子，作到我们全人里面；我们若与这奇妙的原型合作，向祂敞开，祂就要从我们的灵向外扩展到我们心的各部分里─三16～21。
2.　God's way to mass reproduce this prototype is to work His living prototype, the first-born Son, into our entire being; if we cooperate with and open up to this wonderful prototype, He will spread outward from our spirit into all the parts of our heart— 3:16-21.
二　那灵安排我们的环境，使万人、万事与万物都互相效力，叫我们得益处；罗马八章二十八节的“益处”，乃指更多得着基督作到我们里面；生命之灵的律用生命供应我们，以变化我们并将我们模成神长子基督的形像，使我们成为献给神的基督馨香之气─耶四八11，林后二15，歌四16。
B.　The Spirit arranges our circumstances, causing all persons, all matters, and all things to work together for good; the "good" in Romans 8:28 refers to our gaining more of Christ, to our having Him wrought into our being; the law of the Spirit of life supplies us with life to transform us and to conform us to the image of Christ as the firstborn Son of God, making us a fragrance of Christ to God—Jer. 48:11; 2 Cor. 2:15; S. S. 4:16.
三　我们模成神长子的形像，乃是我们的定命，也是神圣生命在我们里面作工的目标；我们照着那在耶稣身上是实际者学了基督，就是在基督这榜样的模子里，模成基督的形像，在复活里接受祂作我们神圣的生命，而在神里面、同着神、为着神、凭着神、并向着神作一切，使神得着荣耀─罗八29，弗一4～5，四20～21，罗十一36。
C.　For us to be conformed to the image of God's firstborn Son is our destiny and the goal of the working of the divine life within us; our learning Christ as the reality is in Jesus is to be molded into the pattern of Christ, conformed to the image of Christ, by taking Him as our divine life in resurrection to do everything in God, with God, for God, by God, and to God for the glory of God—Rom. 8:29; Eph. 1:4-5; 4:20-21; Rom. 11:36.
四　我们被模成，乃是我们在神圣生命上的成熟，借此我们完满的有分于神的神性，而在具有祂的神圣成分并经历祂生机的救恩上，得到具体：
D.　Our conformation is our maturity in the divine life through which we participate in God's divinity in full and are solidified in the possession of His divine element and in the experience of His organic salvation:
1　变化是我们在天然的生命里新陈代谢的改变，成熟乃是我们被那改变我们的神圣生命所充满─林后三18，来六1上，西一28～29。
1.　To be transformed is to be metabolically changed in our natural life; to be mature is to be filled with the divine life that changes us—2 Cor. 3:18; Heb. 6:1a; Col. 1:28-29.
2　生命成熟是被作生命的神所充满，祝福乃是生命的满溢，就是神借着人生命成熟而有的满溢；祝福别人就是将人带到神面前，并将人带进神圣三一的神圣分赐里─民六22～27，林后十三14，彼前三8～9。
2.　Maturity in life is a matter of being filled with God as life, and blessing is the over-flow of life, the overflow of God through the maturity in life; to bless others is to bring them into the presence of God and into the divine dispensing of the Divine Trinity—Num. 6:22-27; 2 Cor. 13:14; 1 Pet. 3:8-9.
五　包罗万有、赐生命、内住的生命之灵的律，正将积极而有能的神圣生命注入我们里面，在我们里面作工，要“基督化”我们，使我们在生命、性情和彰显上，与基督一模一样。
E.　The all-inclusive, life-giving, indwelling law of the Spirit of life is infusing us with the active and energetic divine life, working within us to "Christify" us, to make us exactly the same as Christ in life, nature, and expression.
六　我们可以借着神圣生命的显出，看出人是否享受并经历奏厄，就是神圣的生命─参民六6～9：
F.　We can see whether someone is enjoying and experiencing zoe, the divine life, by the manifestations of the divine life—cf. Num. 6:6-9:
1　那些不肯完全向主敞开、接受祂作生命的光的人，虽然还能用头脑听信息并读圣经，但他们所听的，所读的，不过成了他们定罪别人的张本，批评别人的工具，而自己却一点光都得不着。
1.　Those who are not willing to fully open themselves to the Lord to receive Him as the light of life may still use their mind to listen to messages and read the Bible, but what they hear and read become only a reference for them to judge others, an instrument to criticize others, while they themselves receive not a bit of light.
2　那些向主关闭的人，专会定罪人，批评人，对别人的光景看得很清楚，而对自己的情形却一点不认识；这证明他们完全是在黑暗里！
2.　Those who close themselves to the Lord are experts in judging and criticizing others; they are very clear about others' condition, but they do not know a bit concerning their own condition; this proves that they are entirely in darkness!
3　我们在聚会中是如何听一篇健康、正确的信息，就可以显明在我们的心思里是生命或死亡；我们若喜乐的接受信息，就显明心思里满有生命；然而，我们里面若对信息起怀疑或争论，就显明我们心思里的死亡；听众心思里的生命或死亡，可以供应或杀死讲者的灵。
3.　The way that we listen to a healthy, proper message in a meeting may be a manifestation of life or death in our mind; if we receive the message with joy, this is the manifestation of a mind full of life; however, if we inwardly question and argue with the message, this is a manifestation of death in our mind; the life or death in the minds of the listeners can supply or kill the spirit of the speaking one.
4　我们若满了生命，尽管我们也许没有作什么，但我们这人就会彰显生命，并供应生命给周围的人─约壹五16上。
4.　When we are full of life, although we may not do anything, our being will express life and minister life to those around us—1 John 5:16a.
叁　生命之灵的律乃是基督的律法作为爱的律法─罗八2，加六2，约十三34：
III.　The law of the Spirit of life is the law of Christ as the law of love—Rom. 8:2; Gal. 6:2; John 13:34:
一　神先爱我们，将祂的爱注入我们里面，并且在我们里面产生出爱来，使我们能用这爱爱祂，并爱众弟兄─约壹四19～21。
A.　God first loved us in that He infused us with His love and generated within us the love with which we love Him and the brothers—1 John 4:19-21.
二　保罗在林前十三章所描述的爱，乃是神圣生命的彰显（4～8上）；不仅如此，爱乃是那灵的果子，这事实指明爱的本质必须是那灵（加五22）；我们若没有爱，我们的说话就如同鸣的锣、响的钹，发出声音却没有生命（林前十三1）。─引用经文
B.　The love described by Paul in 1 Corinthians 13 is the expression of the divine life (vv. 4-8a); furthermore, the fact that love is the fruit of the Spirit indicates that the substance of love must be the Spirit (Gal. 5:22); if we do not have love, our speaking is like that of sounding brass and a clanging cymbal, which give sounds without life (1 Cor. 13:1).
三　爱是不嫉妒，不轻易发怒，不计算人的恶，凡事包容，凡事忍耐，比一切存留得更长久，并且是最大的─4～8上，13节。
C.　Love is not jealous, is not provoked, does not take account of evil, covers all things, endures all things, survives everything, and is the greatest—vv. 4-8a, 13.
四　爱的律法必须由生命之灵的律将其实化，使我们能彼此担当重担，成为我们在灵里并凭着灵而行的自然结果（加六2，五16，25）；但我们若满了骄傲，就不能担当别人的重担；这是因为我们自己欺骗自己，自以为是什么，其实我们什么也不是（六3）。─引用经文
D.　The law of love must be substantiated by the law of the Spirit of life so that we may be able to bear one another's burdens as a spontaneous result of our walking in and by the Spirit (Gal. 6:2; 5:16, 25), but if we are filled with pride, we will be unable to bear others' burdens; this is because we deceive ourselves by thinking that we are something when we are nothing (6:3).
五　当爱的律法在我们里面得以发动，我们就自动并自然的成为牧人，有我们父神爱和赦免的心，并我们救主基督牧养和寻找的灵，寻找并找着失去的那只羊─约二一15～17，路十五1～7。
E.　When the law of love is activated within us, we automatically and spontaneously will be shepherds who have the loving and forgiving heart of our Father God and the shepherding and seeking spirit of our Savior Christ, going after and finding the one sheep that is lost—John 21:15-17; Luke 15:1-7.
六　当爱的律法在我们里面得以发动，我们在主里的劳苦就是爱心的劳苦（林前十五58，帖前一3～4）；在其中我们“扶助软弱的人”（徒二十35）并“扶持软弱的人”（帖前五14）；“软弱的人”指那些在灵、魂、体方面软弱，或是在信心上软弱的人（罗十四1，十五1）。─引用经文
F.　When the law of love is activated within us, our labor in the Lord is a labor of love (1 Cor. 15:58; 1 Thes. 1:3-4) in which we "support the weak" (Acts 20:35) and "sustain the weak" (1 Thes. 5:14); the weak refers to those who are weak either in spirit or soul or body or who are weak in faith (Rom. 14:1; 15:1).
七　我们从神所接受的生命乃是爱的生命；基督曾在这世上活出神就是爱的生活，如今祂是我们的生命，使我们能在这世上活出同样爱的生活，与祂所是的一样─约壹三14，五1，二6，四17。
G.　The life that we have received from God is a life of love; Christ lived in this world a life of God as love, and He is now our life so that we may live the same life of love in this world and be the same as He is—1 John 3:14; 5:1; 2:6; 4:17.
八　我们必须是一个被基督的爱冲没并冲激的人；神圣的爱该像大水澎湃冲向我们，迫使我们情不自禁的向祂活着─林后五14。
H.　We must be persons who are flooded with and carried away by the love of Christ; the divine love should be like the rushing tide of great waters toward us, impelling us to live to Him beyond our own control—2 Cor. 5:14.
九　弟兄相爱是旧诫命，也是新诫命：是旧诫命，乃因信徒从基督徒生活的开始就有了；是新诫命，乃因在基督徒的行事为人上，这诫命一再露出新的曙光，一再以新的亮光及新鲜的能力照耀─约壹二7～8，三11，23，参约十三34。
I.　The commandment regarding brotherly love is both old and new: old, because the believers have had it from the beginning of their Christian life; new, because in their Christian walk it dawns with new light and shines with new enlightenment and fresh power again and again—1 John 2:7-8; 3:11, 23; cf. John 13:34.
十　召会生活乃是弟兄相爱的生活（约壹四7～8，约贰5～6，约十五12，17，启三7，弗五2，参犹12上），并且身体在爱里把自己建造起来（弗四16）。─引用经文
J.　The church life is a life of brotherly love (1 John 4:7-8; 2 John 5-6; John 15:12, 17; Rev. 3:7; Eph. 5:2; cf. Jude 12a), and the Body builds itself up in love (Eph. 4:16).
十一　神赐给我们的灵，就是蒙了重生的灵，乃是爱的灵；我们需要有一个火热的爱的灵，以征服今日召会的堕落─提后一6～7，罗十二11。
K.　Our God-given, regenerated spirit is a spirit of love; we need a burning spirit of love to conquer the degradation of today's church—2 Tim. 1:6-7; Rom. 12:11.
十二　“知识是叫人自高自大，惟有爱建造人”；我们可能听了职事的信息，只得了一些知识，就自高自大（林前八1下，参林后三6）；彼此相爱是我们属于基督的表记（约十三34～35）。─引用经文
L.　"Knowledge puffs up, but love builds up"; we may listen to the messages of the ministry and become puffed up with mere knowledge (1 Cor. 8:1b; cf. 2 Cor. 3:6); loving one another is a sign that we belong to Christ (John 13:34-35).
十三　在召会中间好为首，乃与爱众弟兄相对─约叁9：
M.　Loving to be first in the church is versus loving all the brothers—3 John 9:
1　在主工作中的争竞，不仅是雄心的表记，也是骄傲的表记；题到自己的才能、成功、完全和美德，乃是骄傲的一种轻率形态。
1.　Rivalry in the Lord's work is not only a sign of ambition but also a sign of pride; referring to our capacity, success, perfection, and virtue is a careless form of pride.
2　看自己过于所当看的，是骄傲的另一种形态（罗十二3）；自夸、自高、自荣、食图虚荣，都是骄傲丑陋、卑下的表现（加五25～26）。─引用经文
2.　Thinking more highly of ourselves than we ought to think is another form of pride (Rom. 12:3); self-boasting, self-exaltation, self-glorification, and lusting after vainglory are all ugly and base expressions of pride (Gal. 5:25-26).
十四　正如主耶稣舍了祂的魂生命，使我们能得着神圣的生命，我们在实行身体的生活时，也需要舍去我们的魂生命并否认己，以爱弟兄并将生命供应给他们─约壹三16，约十11，17～18，十五13，弗四15～16，29～五2，林后三6，四12～13，十二15，罗十二9～13。
N.　Just as the Lord Jesus laid down His soul-life so that we might have the divine life, we need to lose our soul-life and deny the self to love the brothers and minister life to them in the practice of the Body life—1 John 3:16; John 10:11, 17-18; 15:13; Eph. 4:15-16, 29—5:2; 2 Cor. 3:6; 4:12-13; 12:15; Rom. 12:9-13.
十五　我们需要丧失我们的魂生命，不爱这世界及其享乐；反之，我们应当接受并彰显是爱的神，以此为我们的喜乐、娱乐、消遣和快乐─约壹二15～17，太十六25～26，诗三六8～9，参提后三1～5。
O.　We need to lose our soul-life by not loving the world with its pleasure; instead, taking in God and expressing God as love should be our joy, amusement, entertainment, and happiness—1 John 2:15-17; Matt. 16:25-26; Psa. 36:8-9; cf. 2 Tim. 3:1-5.
十六　在召会生活中，弟兄相爱乃是实际的表现在顾到缺乏圣徒的需要，而没有任何自私的目的或外表自我的显扬；在与缺乏圣徒分享物质的东西时，主生命的恩典连同祂的爱，就在基督身体的众肢体之间涌流，并注入他们里面─约壹三17～18，太六1～4，罗十二13，林后八1～7。
P.　Brotherly love in the church life is expressed practically in our caring for the necessities of the needy saints without any self-serving purpose or outward self-display; in the sharing of material things with the needy saints, the grace of the Lord's life with His love flows among the members of the Body of Christ and is infused into them— 1 John 3:17-18; Matt. 6:1-4; Rom. 12:13; 2 Cor. 8:1-7.
十七　我们住在爱里面，习惯的用神的爱爱人，就履行了我们怀着雄心大志，要讨主的喜悦，并且不会惧怕主再来时会受祂刑罚─约壹四16～18，林后五9～11，太二五21。
Q.　Our abiding in love by habitually loving others with the love of God fulfills our determination to gain the honor of being well pleasing to Him and has no fear of being punished by the Lord at His coming back—1 John 4:16-18; 2 Cor. 5:9-11; Matt. 25:21.
十八　为着建造召会作基督生机的身体，在我们的所是和所作上，爱乃是极超越的路─林前十二31下～十三8上。
R.　Love is the most excellent way for us to be anything or do anything for the building up of the church as the organic Body of Christ—1 Cor. 12:31b—13:8a.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
第十五篇　被神的灵引导，真实并实际的是神的儿子
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
读经：罗一3～4，八2，4，6，9～11，13～15，29，十二2，4～5，林后二10，三18
壹　罗马书中深奥的神圣思想，乃是神成为人，为要使罪人在神完整的救恩里，得蒙救赎、重生、圣别、更新、变化、模成并荣化，而成为神的众子，在生命和性情上与神一样，作基督身体的肢体，使祂得着团体的彰显─八3，一3～4，三24，五10，八14，29～30，十二2，4～5。
贰　按照罗马书，神的福音乃是儿子名分的福音，为着基督身体的实际─一3～4，八14，十二4～5：
一　罗马书解释，四福音所启示个人的基督，如何能成为行传所启示由祂自己和众信徒集体组成之团体的基督─徒九4。
二　保罗在罗马书里给我们看见，神新约的经纶乃是要将罪人作成神的儿子和基督的肢体，构成基督的身体以彰显祂─十二4～5。
三　罗马书中的福音，乃是现今住在信徒里面，作他们主观救主者的福音；神的福音乃是罗马书的主题，论到基督在祂复活后，成了那灵在信徒里面─一1，9，八9～11。
四　神救恩的目的，是要使基督（神的长子）复制在千万信徒（神许多的儿子）里面，使他们成为祂身体的肢体，不是分开而完整的个别单位，乃是活的，有功用的，配搭一起，整体的许多部分─十二4～5。
